Current Commentary

The General Budget for This Fiscal Year Has Been Approved 13

Over the years, our country's national economy has reached an extremely dangerous state. On the one hand, prices are falling and there is overproduction. On the other hand, purchasing is stagnant and unemployment is increasing. In this state of poverty, the hardest hit is probably the country's finances, especially the finances of the central government.

According to the Central News Agency, the national general budget for the 23rd fiscal year has been approved by the Central Political Council. The total revenue and expenditure are each 777 million yuan. By comparing the major revenue and expenditure items of the general budget, we can see that the shadow of the national economic decline has been fully reflected in the country's finances.

First, there is the tightening of the central recurring expenditure. Whether the national defense agencies and other administrative agencies have separately handled special expenditure budgets other than this general budget is something we will temporarily ignore. Just looking at the recurring military expenditure item in the general budget, it seems to be more than 100 million yuan less than the previous year. This is clearly due to the increase in debt expenditure, the substantial return of administrative expenditure to normalcy, and the increase in other expenditure figures. At the same time, the shortage of national recurring revenue is, of course, also a very important reason why this general budget has adopted a tight principle in its figures. Second, there is the transformation of methods for making up for revenue and expenditure. The central financial revenue and expenditure of our country have never been truly balanced or appropriate. In the past five or six years, due to the poverty of the national treasury, the authorities could not avoid the reality of "taking from and helping" the financial markets. As a result, it led to the phenomenon of excessive issuance of public bonds. Accumulated to this day, the expenditure of principal and interest on public bonds increases year by year, reaching a huge amount of about 258 million yuan. The direct impact of excessive issuance of public bonds is, of course, to increase the burden on the financial market and indirectly hinder the development of industry. At the current stage of the national economy, the methods for making up for the inadequacy of financial revenue and expenditure have reached a stage where they must be transformed. The fact that the bureau has already begun a trend of increasing tax policies in this general budget proves that the above statement is not false. As for whether the method of increasing taxes can completely solve the current limitation of inadequate central revenue and expenditure, that is a matter for separate discussion.

Can the policy of increasing taxes really solve the current financial difficulties? Even if the increase in tax revenue can be as estimated, what will its impact be? These are all questions that can be answered after a simple explanation of the content of the tax increase policy. In this general budget, it is estimated that salt tax will increase by 44 million yuan, consolidated tax will increase by 20 million yuan, and customs duties will also increase significantly. In total, taxes will increase by more than 70 million yuan. In terms of the affected commodities, salt is a necessity of life, so increasing taxes only increases the degree of difficulty in life. Although the burden of consolidated tax is said to be the most important for the cigarette industry, the burden borne by the cotton yarn, matches, cement, wheat flour, and other industries accounts for about one-third of the total consolidated tax. As for the changes in customs duty rates, they can affect the cost and price of commodities everywhere. In this way, the target of this tax increase is entirely commodity-based. Therefore, the sales status of commodities is the basis for determining the effectiveness of the tax increase. Our country's current foreign trade is in a state of daily contraction, and the important industries of the country are also in danger of collapse. After the bankruptcy of the countryside, if there is a major drought, it is a big question whether the people's consumption of goods can be expected to increase. This is where we cannot be optimistic about the method of increasing taxes. We believe that at a time when the national economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, the result of increasing taxes will not reduce the crisis in government procurement, whether in terms of production costs or national livelihood. Therefore, we cannot see any method for solving financial difficulties in this general budget.

Drought, Heat, Wind, and Rain in Various Places 14

(Jinan) There has been a severe drought with no rain, and grain prices are rising several times a day. Han Fuqu telegraphed Jiang and Wang, stating that Shandong Province is suffering from extreme heat and drought, and the people are in dire straits. Every time he thinks about it, he forgets to sleep and eat. Wang replied by telegram, saying that he deeply sympathizes with the situation and hopes to be informed of the agricultural situation at any time. (Special Dispatch, 21st) (Tianjin) Neiqiu, Hebei, is suffering from extreme heat, with daily temperatures of 108 degrees Fahrenheit for a week. Several people die of heatstroke every day. On the 18th, as many as eleven women and infants fainted and died. Yongnian County is also suffering from an extraordinary drought. On the 18th and 19th, twenty-three people fainted and died, all due to heatstroke. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

(Tianjin) There has been great heat in Longping County for days. A temple fair was held in Niujiaqiao, which is part of the county, on the 16th, and more than 40 villagers died of heatstroke. The government, fearing an epidemic, immediately ordered the temple fair to be stopped. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

(Tianjin) There has been no rain in Anping County, Hebei, for more than 20 days. More than a thousand acres of crops have withered and died. Farmers in Liucun and Haocun are fleeing to other places for fear of the heat. From the 16th to the 19th, more than 60 men, women, old, and young died of heatstroke, and more than 20 livestock also died of heatstroke. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

(Beiping) The water level in various rivers in Hebei Province is gradually rising, but because the wind and rain are favorable, this year's autumn harvest is expected to be abundant. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

(Tianjin) The Hebei Provincial Government believes that the water level in the Yellow River in southern Hebei is rising, and the flood season is approaching. The levee in Hua County, Henan Province, has not been repaired. If the water level rises, southern Hebei may be in danger of levee failure and inundation. They have telegraphed the Henan authorities to repair it quickly. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

(Tianjin) As of today, the Hebei Provincial Department of Industry has received reports of drought disasters from 40 counties throughout the province. Many seedlings have withered and died. The drought is most severe in Hejian and Cixian, which have had no rain for 30 days. If it does not rain for another 10 days, all the seedlings in the entire county will wither and die. Furthermore, 34 counties throughout the province have reported to the province that the rainfall has been sufficient. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Hurricane Has Reached Inland 15

(Nanjing) According to the Central Meteorological Institute, the hurricane has reached inland, approximately at 119 degrees East longitude and 28 degrees North latitude. It is currently moving north or north-northwest, and its strength is gradually decreasing. The hurricane is expected to change direction and move northeast within the day. (21st Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanchang) The provincial government, considering the severe drought in various counties, has consulted with the Rural Cooperative Association on relief measures, discussing topics such as water diversion for dry land, dry land crops, and water conservancy. However, no concrete solutions have been reached. Qianshan, Yiyang, Hengfeng, and other counties have been bandit-infested areas for a long time and are now suffering from drought and heat, with cholera rampant. The Health Department has taken a large quantity of medicine to prevent and treat the diseases. Hukou, Pengjin, and other counties have also reported drought. In addition, there have been continuous gales. In Jingdezhen, 17 porcelain kilns were destroyed by the wind, and many kiln workers were killed or injured. In Ji'an, many memorial archways and walls were blown down, and hundreds of crows on the banyan trees at the banyan tree wharf were blown into the river. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) When the telegram was sent, there was a heavy rain, as cool as late autumn. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) The Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Meng Guangpeng, inspected the drought situation in Wuchang on the 21st. The Deputy Director of the Water Conservancy Department of the Economic Committee, Zheng Zhaojing, inspected the Jinshui Sluice and Zhanggong Embankment, and will inspect the Jiangxiang Trunk Embankment within the day, stepping up flood prevention efforts. Yichang and Lishan counties reported rainfall, while Huangmei County reported another locust plague. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Qingdao) Due to the hurricane advancing towards Shanghai, all southward and northward ships have been suspended. The Guitian Wheel is anchored at Huangdao. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Zhenjiang) In Zhenjiang, there was a strong wind and rain all day on the 21st, resembling the plum rain season. The weather was as cold as autumn, with the temperature reaching a maximum of only 76 degrees. The evening wind was even stronger, seemingly a precursor to a hurricane. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) The drought in Zhejiang Province has now spread to more than sixty counties. Although some counties in Hangzhou have received rain in recent days, the rainfall has been insufficient and cannot compensate for the prolonged lack of rain. A widespread famine this year is already a fact. The authorities are planning relief measures as a matter of urgency. The Zhejiang Relief Association is not only rushing to raise relief funds but also sending representatives to Beijing on the morning of the 21st to request relief from the Central Relief Committee. (21st Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) It has been阴 rain in Nanjing for days, and the rain continued non-stop on the 21st. The temperature reached a maximum of only 81 degrees, resembling autumn. People felt cold in single-layer clothing. (21st Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) Nanjing experienced strong winds and showers on the 21st, with the temperature dropping to 78 degrees, a difference of more than 30 degrees compared to a few days ago. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) According to a survey by the Nanjing Police Department, during the heatwave period from July 3rd to July 20th, there were 1,067 deaths. Among them, those who died of heatstroke accounted for six-tenths, dysentery and typhoid fever each accounted for one-tenth, and senility and other diseases accounted for two-tenths. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Jiangyin) There were two heavy rains on the morning and noon of the 21st, greatly comforting people's hearts. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Guangzhou) Due to continuous heavy rain in the West River, the water level remains high. Several parts of Wuzhou and Nanning have been flooded. Southwest Airlines announced that flights between Guangzhou and Nanning have been temporarily suspended due to the flooding of the Nanning airfield. Planes flying to Longzhou will only reach Wuzhou for now. It is reported that the water level in the upper reaches of the West River is very high, making navigation difficult and dangerous. (19th Reuters dispatch) (Xiamen) In Xiamen on the 21st, it was cloudy, windy, and rainy all day. It was even worse at night, with the temperature dropping to 78 degrees, a difference of ten degrees from the previous day. The Zhangzhou and Quanzhou areas were also experiencing wind and rain. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Hong Kong experienced showers on the evening of the 20th and heavy rain on the 21st, completely eliminating the heatwave. The thermometer dropped to 80 degrees. (20th Central News Agency dispatch)

Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Revision

Negotiations Proceeding Smoothly 16

(Guangzhou) The Sino-British conference on revising the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway contract, held in Hong Kong, is progressing well. According to non-official sources, the representatives of both sides have reached an agreement on the distribution of the railway's income. China will receive 72 percent, and Britain will receive 28 percent. This plan will be submitted by the representatives of both sides to their respective governments for approval. The Chinese representative stated that the final approval from the Nanjing government is required before the proposals regarding the conference can be announced, and added that everything should be concluded after one or two more meetings. There are still some technical matters to be agreed upon, which have been handed over to the technical advisors of both sides for resolution. It is expected that there will be no need to amend the clauses in this regard. The main issue is actually in the financial aspect. It is expected that the figures agreed upon will be accepted by both sides. The Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway is 110 miles long, and the British section, from Kowloon to Shenzhen, is only 21 miles long. When the railway was opened to traffic in 1911, both sides agreed that the British section would receive 35 percent of the surplus profit. The Chinese representative now argues that the surplus profit of the railway should be distributed according to the mileage of the Sino-British sections. The British side claims that the British section has several tunnels and that the engineering is more significant than the Chinese section, so the surplus profit cannot be distributed according to mileage. (19th Reuters dispatch)

June

Survey of Mortality Rate in Beijing 17

(Nanjing) The Beijing Municipal Government announced on the 21st the survey records for June from the Joint Office of Vital Statistics. A total of 948 deaths were investigated, 516 males and 432 females. On average, about 32 people died per day, with the highest number on the 28th, with 56 people, and the lowest on the 23rd, with 17 people. Infants around one year old accounted for the highest number of deaths, with 292 people. Classified by cause of death, respiratory diseases were the most common, reaching 168 people, tuberculosis 154 people, measles 135 people, gastrointestinal diseases 80 people, diarrhea and enteritis 72 people, febrile diseases 70 people, stroke 46 people, carbuncles 40 people, heart and kidney diseases 36 people, typhoid fever 32 people, dysentery 23 people, puerperal fever 22 people, and other diseases totaled 72 people. (21st Central News Agency dispatch) Chiang Kai-shek in Guling

Receives Generals from Various Quarters 18

◎Chairman Chiang Kai-shek went to the officers' training corps in Guling for a two-day lecture and returned to Guling on the evening of the 19th. He received various generals on the 20th. It is reported that Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, Xia Douyin, and others are staying in Guling for several more days. (20th Central News Agency dispatch)

Implement Joint Office Work 19

The National Government orders the Executive Yuan and the Military Council to take note. (Nanjing) The National Government received a letter from the Central Political Committee approving Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Eastern (1st) telegram, which formulated 14 articles of the Outline of Measures for Joint Office Work of Provincial Governments, and planned to first implement them in the five provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Fujian within the bandit suppression area, requesting review and approval. After the meeting's decision, it was approved for record and the government was instructed to follow it. The National Government has ordered the Executive Yuan and the Military Council to take note. (21st Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) The joint office work of the five provincial governments was approved for record by the Central Political Committee. On the 21st, the National Government instructed the Executive Yuan and the Military Council to take note. (21st Special Dispatch)

Intelligence on Bandit Suppression in Various Areas 20

(Hankou) The main force of the puppet 25th Army, the 12th and 13th divisions, was defeated by Yao Dongfan's and Wu Ke Ren's divisions. They fled to Lingshanchong, Hejiachong, Tiepuji, and Bai'anshan. Wu's division pursued the bandits to Quanting and recovered Zhi'anshan. Yao's division also captured the bandits' nest in Longchi and destroyed more than 20 bandit sheds, and destroyed a puppet military hospital in Yuejiagou. They are currently tracking and suppressing the bandits. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) According to military sources, there have been only minor skirmishes on the Fujian-Western front, with no major battles. The chief of the security regiment, Chen Peiyu, Ma Hongxing, Peng Tang, Chen Linrong, and the second-term military officer training corps Wang Gupan, returned to Xiamen from the province on the 21st. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Fuzhou) It is reported that the main force of the bandits in Shicheng transported their baggage and equipment overnight on the 20th in preparation for retreating to Ruijin. The recovery of the city should be imminent. (21st Special Dispatch)

Xiuping Road Opened to Traffic Yesterday

Ceremony for Liuwan Road Scheduled for the 1st 24

(Nanchang) The Xiuping and Liuwan highways running through Hunan and Jiangxi have been completed. One runs from Xiushui Station on the Nanchang-Xunyang Railway through Longmen to Pingjiang to reach Changsha, and it opened to traffic on the 21st. The other runs from Changsha through Liuyang, Pingxiang, and Wanzai directly to Nanchang and can be reached on the same day. The roadbed has been completed, and sand is being actively laid and station buildings are being constructed along the way. A ceremony for the opening of the entire road is scheduled for the first day of next month. (21st Central News Agency dispatch)

American Missionary Abducted in Pengshui

Smith Arrives in Hankou 25

(Hankou) The American missionary Smith, who was abducted by the communists in Pengshui on June 6, escaped on June 28. He arrived here this morning from Fuzhou on a Yiping boat. According to his statement to a Reuters reporter about the circumstances of the incident, the Pengshui soldiers abandoned the city and fled when the communists were approaching. The bandit leader He Long suddenly attacked the city on the evening of June 8 and captured it without resistance. All the officers left behind were killed. The county magistrate and others escaped by civilian boat. The communists then went to the church, and he was abducted. Two days later, the Sichuan soldiers returned, and He's bandits retreated towards Kui County, taking him with them. On June 28, he and a servant escaped from the detention center while the guarding bandits were asleep. They were quickly discovered, but they were not captured because it was dark. Over the next five days, they experienced many dangers. Fortunately, he had medicine with him and used it to trade with farmers for eggs, beans, and wheat cakes to fill their stomachs. They hid during the day and only dared to travel at night. He was captured by government soldiers three times but was released each time. One night, they stayed at a farmer's house, which was attacked by communists who wanted to kill him. He jumped out of a window on the upper floor and crawled through the rice paddies to escape. His servant shouted for help but was also released and found his master. The master and servant then walked barefoot for a day and a half to reach Kui County, exhausted and hungry. After being interrogated by the military authorities there, he was allowed to return to Pengshui and then set off from Fuzhou to come here. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Tax-Free Purchase of Foreign Rice

Price Survey Required First 26

(Nanjing) Gu Xinyi of the Shanghai Rice Merchants Association submitted a request to the Rural Reconstruction Committee to purchase 750,000 dan of foreign rice tax-free to stabilize rice prices, and to levy a tax of one yuan per dan upon import to establish a food transportation and sales company. The Executive Yuan handed it over to the Ministries of Finance, Industry, and Internal Affairs for joint review. The three ministries believed that it was still difficult to predict the extent of this year's disaster. Although rice prices are currently rising, it is uncertain whether it is necessary to purchase foreign rice, and there is no accurate statistics on the total amount of rice stored in the country. Whether the method of levying one yuan per dan in the midst of tax exemption and designating it for the operation of the food transportation and sales company is appropriate is also under consideration. Therefore, the results of their discussion, it is heard, are (1) Tax reduction and tax exemption cannot be designated for a specific purpose; (2) Tax increase and tax exemption are an overall and universal issue and cannot be reduced or exempted on one side; (3) Whether this case should be handled, and whether tax reduction and tax exemption should be granted, should be discussed after the Ministries of Finance and Industry investigate rice prices and rice reserves. Yesterday, it was submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. (21st Special Dispatch)

Renovating Pinghan Railway

Six Projected Uses 27

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways is renovating the Pinghan Railway and rebuilding the Yellow River Railway Bridge, borrowing 30 million yuan from Shanghai banking circles, which is currently in progress. The person in charge of the liaison is Zhou Zuomin of the Jincheng Bank. In addition to Jincheng and Yanye banks acting as representatives, the Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu will also unite other banks to form a banking consortium to handle it. The issue of collateral is currently being negotiated, and the contract has not yet been signed. The Ministry of Railways has projected six uses: (1) Purchase 500,000 sleepers, (2) Purchase 90,000 tons of steel rails, (3) Replace the southern section of the iron barriers and repair the Yellow River Railway Bridge, (4) Add equipment to the pinyiqi factory, (5) Install long-distance telephones, (6) Repair locomotives and passenger and freight cars. The entire plan is scheduled to be completed within five years. (21st Special Dispatch)

Loan for Yuehan Railway

Organization of the Custody Committee 28

(Nanjing) The Yuehan Railway project, borrowing 3.5 million pounds from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity, equivalent to 24 million yuan in national currency, had been approved earlier. The Ministry of Railways established the Yuehan Railway Loan Custody Committee. The Ministry of Railways appointed Zhai Shaohuang, Zhen Sheng, Chen Qicai from the Boxer Indemnity Association, Hang Liwu, Jiang Lufu from the Ministry of Finance, Pang Songzhou, and Huang Youying from the Audit Department to jointly organize it. This bond will be issued in Shanghai on August 1, with an annual interest rate of six percent and a repayment period of twelve years. (21st Special Dispatch)

Major Fire in Tianjin Yesterday Morning 31

20,000 bales of sheepskin lost in the warehouse. (Tianjin) At 1:00 a.m. this morning, a fire broke out in the warehouse of the Xintai Hing foreign firm on Zhongjie Street in the Tianjin British Concession due to a short circuit. Because the wind was very strong, the fire started in the middle of the night. By the time people noticed, it was already unstoppable. All 30-odd rooms were burned down. Fire brigades from various concessions worked together to put out the fire, which was finally extinguished at 3:00 a.m. 20,000 bales of Xining sheepskin were lost, worth more than 200,000 yuan, making it a rare major fire in Tianjin in recent times. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Last night, a fire broke out in the Yihe Road warehouse of the Xintai Hing foreign firm. The warehouse was filled with wool and burlap sacks. Fire trucks from the British, French, and Italian concessions came to put out the fire, but they were unable to extinguish it immediately. The estimated loss is about 300,000 yuan, of which only a portion was insured against fire. The cause of the fire is unknown. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Qixia Mountain Station

Armed Robbery by Bandits 32

(Nanjing) According to railway sources, dozens of bandits suddenly came to Qixia Mountain Station at 1:00 a.m. on the 21st, carrying weapons and committing robbery. The stationmaster was beaten and injured. They looted for an hour before leaving. Several hundred yuan were lost. The Beijing Station was notified at 8:00 a.m. on the 21st and has sent personnel to investigate and notify the military and police to strictly pursue the fleeing bandits. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Qixia Mountain Station, 20 kilometers from Nanjing, was robbed by armed bandits at 1:00 a.m. on the 21st. The stationmaster was kidnapped, and several hundred yuan in cash were robbed. The stationmaster was soon released and is reported to have been injured. It was reported afterward that only a hundred-odd yuan in paper money were lost. At the time, the bandits were extremely flustered and hurriedly left the station in just a few minutes, fleeing into the mountains. The headquarters has telegraphed Company Commander Jiang at the location to quickly round up the bandits, and a reward has been offered for their arrest. A reward of one hundred yuan will be paid for each captured bandit, so that the case can be solved as soon as possible. (21st Special Dispatch)

He arrived at the Academia Sinica on the morning of the 21st and met with Li Shuhua and others to discuss everything. According to Xu's statement to reporters, the archaeological work in Shaanxi this time has yielded excellent results and made many contributions to scholarship. It has now temporarily come to an end, and he plans to continue his work in the autumn. The antiquities transported to Beiping will be sorted out first, and an exhibition will be held around the end of the month. (21st Central News Agency dispatch)

China Eastern Railway Resumes Traffic 34

(Harbin) The China Eastern Railway between Changchun and Harbin, which was suspended on the 17th due to the tracks being washed away by the flood, has resumed normal traffic today after being repaired day and night. The water level of the Songhua River is still rising. This morning, the Chenhe (transliteration) embankment breached. Hundreds of workers rushed to the scene to use flour bags to hold sand to block the breach to prevent Daoli from being flooded. (21st Reuters dispatch) (Beiping) The statement that traffic to Siberia had been suspended due to flooding in Manchuria is now known to be inaccurate. Although railway traffic in northern Manchuria has been obstructed by the floods, traffic to Siberia is operating as usual. It has been found that in the flooded area of Manchuria, between Changchun and Harbin, north- and south-bound trains stop there and passengers are transferred by motorboat. The trains operate as usual during the day, but night trains are temporarily suspended. This arrangement does not hinder passengers departing from Tianjin via Siberia at all. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Ningxia to Dig New Canals 37

(Beiping) According to a Baotou dispatch, Kong Xiangxi went to Ningxia to inspect and agreed with Ma Hongkui to dig a large canal along the slope of the Helan Mountains, called the Tang Canal, from east to west to Shizuishan and into the river. Another large canal will be dug along the vicinity of the Yellow River, called the Yellow River Canal, also from southeast to northwest to Shizuishan and into the river. The two canals will total more than 500 li in length and will be collectively called the Rongting Canal. The designs have been drawn, and the central government has allocated 200,000 yuan to be excavated by soldiers. The funds have been allocated and excavation will begin soon. It is expected to be completed this year. (21st Special Dispatch)

Beiping City Reforms Local Self-Government 38

(Beiping) Beiping City's self-government was originally divided into 15 districts and 462 neighborhoods, and the district and neighborhood chiefs were specially selected. Recently, due to poor management, the City Government's Self-Government Supervision Office, based on the eighth item of the Internal Affairs Department's revised and improved explanation of the principles of local self-government, merged the self-governing neighborhoods in the urban area into 119 neighborhoods, and changed the district and neighborhood chiefs to an appointment system. It was announced on the 20th and implemented from the 21st. Sun Baorong, Director of the Supervision Office, received the Beiping press at 11:00 a.m. on the 21st to report on the reorganization and merger process. The City Council believes that the City Government's reorganization of the self-governing districts has a significant impact on the future of self-government, and since the case was not submitted for discussion in advance, it cannot agree. It has issued a consultation to the City Government for investigation and consideration on the 21st in accordance with the law. (21st Central News Agency dispatch)

Busts Counterfeiting Operation 39

(Tianjin) At No. 3 Jiyoshino Street, Tianjin Japanese Concession, a Polish woman, Karola Svorova, and a British couple, the Gannimos, were found to be counterfeiting banknotes from the Bank of Communications, the Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and the Citibank. It was discovered by the Tianjin French Concession Police Bureau at 2:00 p.m. on the 21st, and they were arrested in cooperation with the Japanese police. (21st Special Dispatch)

Daming Garrison Reassigned to the 51st Army 40

(Tianjin) The cavalry third division of the He Zhuguo army, led by Guo Fengyang, stationed in Daming, has recently been ordered by the Military Council to be reassigned to the 51st Army, led by Yu Xuezhong, and will remain in its original defense. (21st Special Dispatch)

Opinions on Governing Mongolian Leagues 41

Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs Expands Budget

Overseas Information Network 54

(Tokyo) As a result of yesterday's Ministry of Foreign Affairs' ministerial meeting, it was decided to incorporate a newly established fee of 2.3 million yen for the International Culture Bureau into the new budget, implement a new cultural affairs officer system, appoint suitable personnel to major embassies in key countries, and dispatch information offices to various locations to fully complete the overseas information network. In order to further enhance the functions of both, it was decided to spend 130,000 yen to establish Japanese research institutes in Paris and New York to promote foreign understanding of Japan and strengthen external cultural work. (21st, Domei News Agency dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs' budget for the next fiscal year is currently being compiled amidst widespread attention. The issue of a major expansion of the Cultural Affairs Department, aimed at assisting diplomacy during times of emergency, has been decided upon with internal support. The total budget is estimated at 3.5 million yen, and the plan's contents are as follows:

(1) Establishment of an International Culture Bureau (800,000 yen). This plan is essentially a major expansion of the current Cultural Affairs Department, aiming to achieve the purpose of introducing a unified Japanese culture. (2) Establishment of cultural diplomats, the highest-level agency for introducing culture and engaging in practical activities. Resident offices will be established in five locations: London, Paris, Berlin, New York, and Rio de Janeiro. Japanese Cultural Research Institutes will be specifically established in the two cities of Paris and New York. (3) Two million yen from the cultural affairs budget will be used to establish new Japanese cultural studies programs at major universities in Europe and the United States, and to exchange university professors. (4) Support the work of the International Cultural Promotion Association. (21st, Japan United Press dispatch)

British Navy's Claim

Unlimited Construction of Light Cruisers 55

Vast territories require self-defense but must not endanger other countries. (London) The Navy League today issued a statement, insisting that the British government maintain complete freedom regarding the issue of light and heavy cruisers at future naval conferences. From this perspective, if the British delegation uses this statement as a basis for negotiation, then what the naval conference can limit will only be the number and tonnage of battleships. Regarding the battleship issue, the British Navy League's statement hinted that Britain only wants to maintain a balance of power with other countries. The statement further stated that Britain's overseas territories are vast, and in order to fully protect the sources of supply, the absolute right to build light cruisers is a necessity. The position of the British Empire is quite unique and will never endanger other countries. Therefore, no country should have any objection to the freedom of action that Britain requests for self-defense. (21st, National Telegraph dispatch)

(Washington) The Washington Star published a commentary stating that if Italy's plan to build two 35,000-ton battleships is implemented, France will have to declare the Washington Naval Treaty null and void in order to meet the necessary requirements. This is because, to maintain France's security, it is necessary for the French navy to be equivalent to the combined strength of the Italian and German navies. The new French Dunkerque-class warships are only enough to counter the pocket battleships built by Germany. If Italy builds new ships and reaches the tonnage limits stipulated by the Washington Treaty, then France will inevitably follow Italy's example. If that happens, France will have to abandon the Washington Treaty because, according to the Washington Treaty, Italy can still build 70,000 tons of new ships, and so can France. Now France has built several Dunkerque-class battleships, totaling 52,000 tons, leaving only 18,000 tons remaining. Even if the old and obsolete battleship France is removed from consideration, it can still add 22,000 tons. However, to be equal to the tonnage of Italy's new battleships, it is still 30,000 tons short. It is now heard that the British Admiralty is strongly urging Mussolini to cancel the plan to build 35,000-ton battleships, because the British plan advocates reducing the tonnage of each battleship from 35,000 tons to 25,000 tons. The Italian plan contradicts this British proposal. In addition, the British Admiralty believes that Mussolini's announcement of the plan to build battleships is deliberately creating a false impression, intending to obtain equal naval power with France at the next naval conference, and then allow the abandonment of this shipbuilding plan, because this plan will still be a dead letter at that time, and the construction of two 35,000-ton battleships requires 70 million US dollars, which Italy does not have the financial resources to do. (20th, Havas dispatch)

German Newspaper Comments on the Value of the Eastern European Pact

Russia Wants to Eliminate Worries in the Rear to Devote Full Strength to Japan 56

(Berlin) The Berlin Börsen-Zeitung published an important essay on its front page today, stating the relationship between the Eastern European Pact and the Far Eastern situation. The newspaper declared that this extraordinary pact, as advocated by France and Soviet Russia, is actually related to the Far Eastern situation, and all the key points are particularly related to Japan. The newspaper also said that, from Soviet Russia's perspective, this pact and its relationship with France can be approved because its purpose is that Soviet Russia, given that a conflict with Japan is inevitable in the future, has to work hard to consolidate the rear in order to avoid being attacked from both sides. This is something everyone knows. If this pact is completed, then Soviet Russia's plan will be successful, and it will no longer have to worry about the rear. However, there is still an important point, that is, this goal cannot be achieved without the practical assistance of France. Furthermore, from Japan's perspective, after this pact is established, it will have the following effects: The countries that signed the Eastern European Pact, including the Baltic states, Poland, Germany, and Czechoslovakia, will guarantee that Soviet Russia will not be attacked in the rear when a war occurs in the Far East. In addition, in the Franco-Russian treaty, France has also clearly guaranteed that each signatory country must fulfill its promises. Therefore, France in this position is no less than a guardian of Soviet Russia, enabling Soviet Russia to devote all its efforts eastward without having to worry about its European neighbors stepping on its toes. Therefore, the Eastern European agreement is greatly beneficial to Soviet Russia, allowing it to focus its full strength on dealing with Japan. Therefore, from Germany's perspective, all disputes involving the Russo-Japanese conflict, whether direct or indirect, must be avoided. (20th, National Telegraph dispatch)

Three Caucasian Ethnic Groups

Plan to Secede from Russia and Become Independent 59

Signing a Joint Defense Pact

(Geneva) The three ethnic groups of the Caucasus region, Azerbaijan, North Caucasus, and Georgia, were formerly under the jurisdiction of Imperial Russia. After the Russian Revolution, they established Soviet republics and were incorporated into the Soviet Union. However, Caucasians abroad are still seeking to break away from the Soviet Union and become independent. The Georgian News Agency here recently released a message stating that representatives of the three Caucasian ethnic groups have recently signed a convention, the content of which is as follows: The signatory Azerbaijan, North Caucasus, and Georgian ethnic groups believe that complete independence is an indispensable condition for the development of all ethnic groups. Therefore, they have jointly decided that, in order to achieve this goal, they should unite the strength of all Caucasian ethnic groups and unify command. The convention consists of six articles, stipulating the methods for Caucasian ethnic groups to break away from Russian rule and organize a joint army for joint defense. The political system adopted by the Caucasian ethnic groups will be the "Caucasian Federation." Article 6 of the convention stipulates that the Armenian ethnic group is allowed to join this convention, and it is expected that Armenia will definitely join. (21st, Havas dispatch)

North African Boundary Treaty 60

Italian Ambassador to Britain Explains the Contents (London) Italy recently signed treaties with Britain and Egypt regarding the boundary affairs of Libya (Italian territory in North Africa) and Sudan. British Ambassador to Italy Sir Drummond recently explained the contents of the boundary treaty to the press, briefly stating that the boundary line between Libya and Sudan is stipulated to start from the intersection of 25 degrees west longitude and 22 degrees north latitude, southward to the intersection of 20 degrees north latitude, turning westward to 24 degrees west longitude (Greenwich area), and then southward to the border with French territory. The British and Egyptian governments give up all claims to the land west and north of this line, and the Italian government does not make any claims to the land east and south of the boundary line. (20th, Havas dispatch)

However, the Prime Minister admitted that he could not speak this language. The Prime Minister will live a simple life among fishermen in Nova Scotia, avoiding the burden of political affairs as much as possible, and will stay here for about half a month. After the Announcement of the Japanese Political Platform

Criticisms from All Sides 62

The Seiyukai compares it to a menu, and the financial community calls it a painted signboard. (Tokyo) Various factions have criticized the Okada Cabinet's political platform and policies. The Minseito Party said that it can be seen from this that the new cabinet does not take extremes and implements the so-called moderate policy of President Wakatsuki. Therefore, it first expresses its approval of this point. The Seiyukai said that it only displays a beautiful menu, but there is actually nothing there. Words such as "consideration" and "reflection" appear repeatedly, and the evidence of no fixed opinions and no direction is clearly visible. The National Alliance said that it is nothing more than a list of political common sense. If only judged by words, it can get 100 points, but abstract words alone cannot be used to make a decision of approval or disapproval. The House of Peers said that the people expect the cabinet change to be accompanied by a declaration of a thorough policy to overcome the national crisis, so as to refresh the hearts of the people of the world. Now, looking at its policies and political platform, it is doubtful whether it can carry out thorough politics. However, there is only hope for the government's efforts and monitoring of its actions. (21st, Domei News Agency dispatch)

(Tokyo) The financial community is very disappointed with the new cabinet's political platform, because its content is too abstract. The general opinion is that with the crisis imminent and the military budget bound to expand, it is said that we must seek a balance between livelihoods and revenues and expenditures. With no clue yet on emergency silkworm farming countermeasures, it is said that we must open up the economy of agricultural and mountain villages. All of this is difficult to achieve. Even its so-called establishment of a comprehensive industrial policy is currently only an ideal. Without seeing the facts in the future, it is just a painted signboard. Since no new flavor has been discovered, it is only waiting for its future concretization to summarize. (21st, Domei News Agency dispatch)

Therefore, some cabinet members complained. Therefore, at the next Five Ministers' Conference, after Ministers Osumi and Hirota report on the matters that were not completed last time, it will be dissolved immediately. Italian-Japanese Trade Competition 68

A US United Press correspondent in Rome learned from official sources that the threat of Japanese commercial competition is gradually being felt here, and Italy's export trade is inevitably suffering a major blow, especially in raw silk and cotton textiles. These products account for a large portion of Italy's foreign trade. Cotton textiles account for 30% of Italy's export trade. The domestic market has not yet been affected by the competition of Japanese goods. Businessmen here say that, with regard to raw silk, Italy can still compete with Japanese goods in terms of quality, but it feels no match for cheap raw silk. Two years ago, the low price of Indian cotton textiles had a great impact on Italy. Italy has suffered annual losses in the markets of India and the Dutch East Indies. Recently, the threat of Japanese industrial and commercial invasion has spread almost all over the world, but it has not had much impact on Italy itself. However, Italy's trade with the Far East, Near East, South America, and Africa has been greatly affected. (21st, National Telegraph dispatch)

German Government

Controls the National Textile Industry 69

(Berlin) The government today ordered that the entire textile industry be under the strict control of the Minister of Economic Affairs. All wool, cotton, and other fibers will be strictly distributed and issued to various factories. Any uneven distribution will be corrected. Each factory will work 36 hours per week to avoid unemployment due to a shortage of raw materials. However, factories that manufacture export products are excluded. It is also forbidden to build new factories or expand old factories. Manufacturers can revise prices or increase world selling prices due to increased costs, but those who try to make huge profits will be severely punished. The Minister of Economic Affairs has the power to fine up to 500 marks and close factories. As a result of the new order, Germans will have to pay higher prices for clothes and textiles in the future, and the German textile industry, which was already depressed, will now have to be subject to the authorities' crackdown, which may lead to further decline. (20th, Reuters dispatch)

Austrian Finances Escape Difficulties 70

Vienna Today, the authorities announced that the government is no longer responsible for the Credit Bank, which caused a great shock among the people here, because the bank is one of the largest in Austria. Then it was learned that it was because the bank's position was stable and did not need government protection, so this announcement was made. As a result, people's hearts were greatly settled. The proclamation stated that the government, at the request of the bank, no longer guarantees the deposits held by the bank because the bank's position is solid. It is said that the bank's transformation from weakness to solidity is actually a victory for the Dollfuss government's finances. An Austrian financial authority commented on this news, saying that Austria has now escaped from the pawnshop. (20th, Reuters dispatch)

French Political Turmoil Developing 71

Radical Party Executive Committee Meeting Acknowledges that Tardieu's Testimony Contains Strategic Political Purpose, but Only the Prime Minister's Personal Mediation Can Save the Situation (Paris) At 2:00 PM today, former Prime Minister and Radical Party member Edouard Herriot met with Radical Party leader Herriot. At 3:00 PM, cabinet members belonging to the Radical Party and members of the party's Executive Committee held a meeting. Edouard Herriot did not participate. After the Executive Committee adjourned the meeting, it issued a communique stating, "The Executive Committee has considered the situation caused by Tardieu's testimony to the Stavisky Affair Investigation Committee. This Committee has unanimous confidence in the Radical Party cabinet members of the current cabinet." The Radical Party cabinet members and Executive Committee members discussed for an hour and unanimously believed that Tardieu's testimony had a partisan strategic political purpose and that the Radical Party cabinet members should properly respond to it. It was also believed that only Prime Minister Doumergue has the right to judge Tardieu's intentions in his testimony and the results that may occur. (20th, Havas dispatch)

(Paris) The political turmoil is now developing. Today, Radical Party cabinet members and the Radical Party Executive Committee held a meeting and unanimously believed that Tardieu's intervention before the Stavisky financial corruption case investigation committee was political in nature. Therefore, the Radical Party cabinet members must be prepared to deal with the political consequences of this move and believe that the cabinet meeting must be chaired by the Prime Minister in order to make the necessary resolutions on this major case. Now Doumergue should be invited to return to Beijing next week to preside over the cabinet meeting. At the same time, the cabinet has decided to send Minister of Justice and Deputy Prime Minister Chiron to Tollefeille to report all the circumstances to Doumergue and discuss with him the matter of holding a cabinet meeting next week with him in the chair. Everyone hopes that Doumergue's arbitration can save the cabinet turmoil. (20th, Reuters dispatch)

San Francisco Returns to Normal

Center of US Labor Unrest Shifts North 72

Strikes in Seattle and Minneapolis Clash with Police. San Francisco The general strike in San Francisco has ended. Except for 13,000 longshoremen who are still on strike, 150,000 workers have resumed work. Therefore, the ports of Seattle and Portland are now the center of the labor unrest on the Pacific coast. (According to the Portland Strike Strategy Committee, it was decided yesterday that if the governor orders the National Guard to come to the area, they will prepare to start a general strike.) Harry Bridges, chairman of the San Francisco longshoremen's strike guidance committee, recently declared that after the general strike in all industries, the status of the longshoremen is becoming more and more solid, which has never been seen before. From now on, he will fight to the end to obtain supervision of new workers. (20th, Havas dispatch)

San Francisco Strikers in San Francisco and Oakland are now gradually returning to work, but the center of the labor unrest has shifted to Minneapolis today. Truck drivers there are creating disturbances, and 35 people have been shot and wounded, which is a serious situation. 3,500 National Guardsmen have been ordered to enter the city to maintain order and security. Governor Olson is considering whether to issue a declaration of martial law, but unless the situation worsens, the governor may not implement this emergency plan. The riots started when police escorted a truck loaded with groceries through the blockade area. Strikers saw it and rushed over in empty trucks. Their momentum was fierce. The police were unprepared, so they fired shots into the air as a warning, but the strikers ignored it and got out of the cars together, rushing directly to the loaded truck, trying to drag out the driver. Seeing that the police were outnumbered, they fired live ammunition at the crowd, and both sides fought each other, injuring many people, including several policemen. Riots also occurred in Seattle. Strikers attacked non-striking transporters with bayonets. The police quickly used tear gas to defend them, and the rioters retreated. Twenty of the strikers were gassed by tear gas, and four policemen were also beaten by the strikers with sticks. Those who sympathized with the strikers even wanted to use machine guns and small blossoming bombs, but this plan has been foiled by the police. The situation in San Francisco is still quiet. The strike has ended, and food is being transported in in a steady stream. The theaters have reopened, and all traces of the labor unrest are now gradually disappearing. Even those who sympathize with the strike have resumed work. Waterfront workers have not yet resumed normal work, but it is hoped that it will be resolved soon through arbitration. Portland shipowners have suffered heavy losses due to the longshoremen's strike, so they still want to proceed with their plan to open the port for trade. The situation there is quite complicated. The National Guard is prepared to take action to suppress any riots that occur when the shipowners implement their plan, but the union has threatened that if troops are stationed on the waterfront, a general strike will be implemented. The National Guard is currently stationed several miles away from the city. The strikers claim that the shipowners are afraid that a fair arbitration will result in a ruling unfavorable to the shipowners, so they now want to force the port to open. (20th, Reuters dispatch)

Longshoremen Are Isolated 73

The longshoremen's and maritime workers' strike in San Francisco was dealt a major blow today because the truck drivers have resolved to resume work and have already loaded and transported the cargo now being unloaded by the shipping companies. This action by the truck drivers has made the longshoremen's strike completely ineffective, because the loading and unloading of cargo on the docks all depends on the truck drivers for transportation. Previously, they refused to transport it, so the transportation business was interrupted. Today, they have resumed work as a result of detailed discussions between the government mediation committee and the truck drivers' union. Although the longshoremen and sailors are still on strike, it is expected that there will be no hope. Today, San Francisco's industry and commerce are gradually returning to normal, and another 150,000 workers have also resumed work. The truck drivers in Oakland have also resolved to resume work, but they still refuse to transport goods to the docks in San Francisco and Oakland. The San Francisco longshoremen, seeing the situation, may completely fail and lose their jobs. Therefore, there is a possibility of expelling radical leaders. The Maritime Workers' Union still declares that it will not stop until the goal of officially recognizing the union is achieved. The police and the "Anti-Communist Squad" are still searching for communist organizations everywhere, and the number of communists arrested has reached 350. There is even overcrowding in the prison, so some of the prisoners have to sleep on the floor. (20th, National Telegraph dispatch)

Extreme Faction Discouraged 74

The longshoremen's union of San Francisco voted today, with 1,338 votes in favor of returning to work and 285 votes against. Therefore, the strike has now officially ended. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

More than 70% of the striking workers in San Francisco returned to work today. The president of the transport workers' union stated that the longshoremen's vote was enough to discourage the extremist leaders of the striking workers who opposed mediation, such as the Australian, Bailey. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

Seattle Mayor Smith, believing that Police Chief Howard's personal leadership of the police to attack dockworkers allowed capitalist forces to disrupt the strike, ordered his dismissal today. Howard had led 300 police officers to attack workers, resulting in severe injuries to three people on each side. The workers were driven back by the police using tear gas and revolvers, allowing the capitalist’s cargo trucks to pass through. (National News Agency dispatch, 20th)

Transfer of Tianjin Japanese Police Chief 76

He Shangping Arrives in Jinan

Discussing Methods to Improve Shandong Silk 77

According to He, special attention will be paid to Shandong autumn cocoons this year. The committee will set up two guidance centers in Shandong, sending technicians with medicines to Shandong for preliminary experiments. The plan to improve Shandong silk will rely on the combined efforts of the Economic Committee, the Shandong Provincial Government, and the banking sector. Proposal to Improve Rickshaw Pullers' Treatment 85

(Guangzhou) Today, the municipal government meeting passed a resolution to improve the treatment of rickshaw pullers. This proposal was jointly submitted by the Finance Bureau, Education Bureau, and Social Affairs Bureau, stipulating that 20% of the rickshaw tax collected will be used in the future to build a rickshaw puller hospital. Rickshaw companies must provide rickshaw pullers with raincoats and rain hats and are prohibited from demanding anything from the rickshaw pullers. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

66.75

North China Diplomacy After Traffic Opens 105

The entire issue remains unresolved, Huang Fu's journey north will take time, customs offices are actively being established at various ports, both sides are preparing to discuss the war zone issue. Beijing communication, North China diplomacy, since the opening of traffic, seems to have made progress on the surface, but the entire issue has not been resolved. The Japanese, harboring aggressive intentions, are pressing us step by step. Their desires are insatiable. To seek a complete solution, various forms of constraints and prohibitions are present, creating obstacles. Moreover, the Japanese demands are excessive, making it difficult for both sides to reach a compromise. The difficulties within are imaginable. According to people from South China, Huang Fu, who is responsible for North China diplomacy, does not have a passive attitude. However, since taking on the responsibility of going north with the intention of "jumping into the fire" last year, he has been working hard and enduring grievances. For over a year, he has only created this situation. At this time, within the country, public opinion is divided on him. Coupled with constraints from various parties, frequent interference, he cannot smoothly implement the pre-planned measures in his heart. Externally, he is dealing with cunning and sly enemies, exhausting his efforts to cope. Looking forward and backward, he is surrounded by thorns. Without a comprehensive plan and overall solution, it is difficult to act as Feng Fu again. During his two secret meetings with Chiang in Hangzhou, no decision was reached. Chiang, seeing the smooth progress of bandit suppression and being overwhelmed with military affairs, urgently needed to return to Jiangxi to preside over matters. Therefore, he instructed Huang to stay temporarily at Mogan Mountain and discuss the matter at length later. Recently, calls from all sides urging Huang to go north are extremely loud. In addition to sending Vice Minister Tang Youren to meet with Huang to discuss everything in detail, Wang also intends to personally go to Hangzhou to meet with Huang. It is said that Huang has no preconceived notions about his personal position, but he must seek a proper solution before going north, so his departure date is difficult to determine.

Various issues planted by the Tanggu Truce have not been resolved due to Japan's barbarity, leading to negotiations almost every day for the past year. When the authorities signed the Tanggu Truce, time was pressing, and they had no choice. Initially, there was no room for foresight, leading to the planting of many seeds of entanglement. Later, when negotiations began, no comprehensive solution was determined, resulting in inevitable failures and losses in responding to situations as they arose. Since the settlement of the traffic issue, the important issues attached to the truce have been resolved, and the survival or abolition of the truce has become a problem. The Japanese hold different views on abolishing the ceasefire agreement, and this matter is unlikely to be resolved soon. There are currently many local issues in progress and awaiting negotiation. One is the establishment of customs offices at various ports. The Japanese have expressed their agreement on this matter. The Ministry of Finance has sent Gao Yuanji, Zhang Yongnian, and others to actively proceed in Beijing. However, Japanese troops have not completely withdrawn from various ports, and considerable procedures are required before establishment. In addition, the issue of war zones, such as receiving Malanyu, war zone security forces, and restraining Japanese and Korean vagrants, has also become a local entanglement. Shibayama, the military attaché of the Japanese embassy, went from Beijing to Changchun a few days ago to study the negotiation policy with the Kwantung Army authorities, preparing to negotiate with our side. Regarding this matter, our side did not formally discuss it before Shibayama left Beijing, only officials in charge such as Yin Rugeng and Tao Shangming exchanged opinions privately. A formal solution must wait until Huang Fu goes north. (18th) Yutian Security Force

Demands Replacement of Commander 106

- Shi Yousan Manipulates from Behind -

- Han Dianbang is Incompetent and Weak -

Tianjin Communication, the Yutian Security Force, reduced to 1,000 men and renamed the War Zone Special Police Force, has been implemented since mid-April when Yin Rugeng went to implement the reduction by provincial order. On May 1st, the newly appointed commander Han Dianbang took office. On the surface, it seems resolved. Because the news is silent, outsiders believe that there is nothing wrong. However, the hidden dangers lurking within have not been eliminated, and the disobedience and arrogance of various units remain the same. Brewing up until recently, the various captains jointly telegraphed the province requesting the removal of Commander Han Dianbang. After the incident occurred, the province telegraphed Yutian County Magistrate Chen Baosheng to investigate the truth nearby and report it for disposal, and telegraphed Gu Rugeng to go to Yutian to resolve it at the right time. Yin has already left Beijing on the 18th of this month. The reason why the captains of the security force demanded the removal of Han Dianbang is that two of Han's followers, at the beginning of the month, used weapons to rob a wealthy household in the county seat, and were caught by Sun, the battalion commander of Han's unit. Thus, they used it as an excuse to drive Han away, accusing Han of protecting his followers, robbing civilians, and failing to manage his subordinates, and lacking command ability. They must choose another capable person as an example for the entire team. The province replied, ordering the two captured followers to be sent to the province for interrogation, but they were delayed in sending the case, quite intending to keep it as evidence of crime and would not send it to the province unless Han Dianbang was removed. As for Ji Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong, originally after commissioning Han Dianbang as commander, he wanted to use a quick knife to cut through the mess and reorganize the unit, even if it was inconvenient to proceed with the reduction, he would also cut off the unit's contact with Shi Yousan, but Han lacked this courage, and was extremely incompetent and weak, controlled by his subordinates, and instead covered up to his superiors in order not to offend his unit, thus allowing his subordinates to become powerful. Sun, the first battalion commander of the unit, was a former subordinate of Shi Yousan, and was exceptionally arrogant, colluding with Inspector Zhang Futian. In addition to the monthly pay requisitioned by the province, the rest were free to act. Shi Yousan also paid a certain amount of subsidy every month to make the unit not forget its roots and keep it for future use. Therefore, the province ordered the unit to reduce the number to 1,000 men, but in reality, it contained more than 1,800 to 1,900 men. If guns and pay were insufficient, Shi Yousan supplemented them. In name, it was a security force, but in fact, it was a group raised by traitors. Special Agent Captain Feng Shouchuan was originally a major bandit in Shandong, and his unit was even more unruly. Although his relationship with Shi Yousan was not deep, he was selfish and wanted to be the commander himself, driving away Han Dianbang. The purpose was the same as Sun's, so his name was also listed in the telegram demanding Han's removal. Because the province believed that the unit relied on the war zone as a barrier and refused to obey orders, fearing that it would cause more serious problems, it was extremely hateful, but there was no way to take measures, so it only used comfort. Han Dianbang's removal is therefore an inevitable trend. The date of the announcement will depend on the results of the investigation. Yesterday, it was heard that Ma, an adjutant of Shi Yousan's unit, had transferred from Tangshan to Yutian, bringing Shi's order to give some instructions to the unit. It is predicted that after Han's dismissal, the successor commander will not be pushed by the unit itself. (19th)

Jinan Cracks

Follow-up Interrogation of Fake Organization Case 107

Feng Yuxiang said it was done by Zhang Zongchang's remnants. Jinan Communication, the special investigation team of the military law office of the 3rd Route Army Headquarters, cracked a large-scale reactionary military organization near Wangguanzhuang and Dahuaishu in Xinzhuang on the 14th of this month. The case has been handed over to the military law office of the headquarters for trial. Since the case was cracked, there has been much speculation in society. Some people even suspected that the case was related to Feng Yuxiang, which is absolutely incorrect. The reporter interviewed Feng at the Five Sages Temple in Mount Tai. According to Feng's statement, "I also learned from the newspapers about the fake military organization cracked by the 3rd Route Army reported in the Jinan newspapers. Judging from its content, it is just a kind of disguised fraud. They are all Zhang Zongchang's remnants who cannot make a living and came up with a way to borrow the name to swindle and sell appointments to deceive the money of the ignorant who want to be officials. It seems to have no other effect. Yesterday (18th), Tong from Jinan Mayor Wen came and also talked about this matter and saw the stocks. According to the speculation of most people, they all believe that they are scattered soldiers and ruffians who are extremely bored, using very little capital to print commissions and be able to exchange them for a lot of compensation. Such things are not worth the laughter of the knowledgeable." (19th)

Telegraphs Beijing to Report Disaster Situation 108

Severe disaster areas reach more than 30 counties, please quickly allocate large sums of money for relief. Hankou Communication, the Hubei Provincial Relief Association, connected the Central Relief Commission's telegram, ordering to investigate and report the disaster situation in various counties in order to coordinate relief. On the 20th, a telegram was sent to Beijing to report and request the allocation of large sums of money for relief. The telegram said, "Urgent, Nanjing Central Relief Commission Junjian, Xiao Yi Er telegram received. As of now, according to reports from various counties in Hubei, the counties with the most severe floods include Tianmen, Zhongxiang, Qianjiang, Jiangling, Hanchuan, Mianyang, Lishan, Tongcheng, Chongyang, Xiangyang, Yun County, etc. The counties with the most severe drought include Wuchang, Guangji, Huang'an, Huangmei, Puqi, Xishui, etc. Personnel have been dispatched or telegrams sent to the counties to investigate in detail. Other dikes and defenses in counties such as Jingshan, Jianli, Zhijiang, Hanyang, Daye, and Shishou are being supervised for emergency protection and are not yet out of danger. The counties most severely affected by bandits include Huang'an, Macheng, Yangxin, Tongshan, Lichuan, Hefeng, Lishan, Chongyin, and Tongcheng, etc., which have been ravaged by bandits for several years, and the number of refugees awaiting food is countless. More disaster reports continue to be received in recent days. In addition to submitting details separately, we respectfully report by telegram first and pray for the quick allocation of large sums of money for relief. The Hubei Civil Affairs Director and Relief Association Chairman Meng Guangpeng humbly kowtows", (20th)

North Jiangxi

Jiuxing Xiuping Road Completed and Opened to Traffic 109

| Ceremonies Have Been Held Successively |

Raozhou Communication, Xingzi County in North Jiangxi (ie, the old Nankang Prefecture) is located on the back of Mount Lu and faces Poyang Lake. Although it holds the key point of the Gan River shipping route, it has not been able to occupy an important position in commercial transportation because there are Raozhou above, Wucheng in the middle, and Jiujiang below. The city is depressed, showing the tattered economic situation of the people. Especially land transportation is extremely inconvenient. From Xunyang to Nankang, travelers used to detour through the rugged Mazhong Cen in the mountains to reach there. The freight of daily necessities for the residents is extraordinarily heavy, and sometimes there is a shortage of porters, and there is no way to supply them. The Road Department of the Construction Department believes that Guling is a resort for Chinese and foreigners, and Xingzi Bailudong is also a famous site where Zhu Zi lectured on scriptures. In Jiangxi, which is striving for construction here, it is even more necessary to improve the traffic on this road. Therefore, a plan for construction was immediately drawn up, ordering the two counties of Jiujiang and Xingzi to rush to build it within a limited time to benefit merchants and travelers. After receiving the order, the county started construction this spring. Since the start of construction, the project has progressed very quickly. All the earthwork, bridges, and water pipes on the entire road were completed last month, and the opening ceremony was held on the 5th of this month. As soon as the road surface is slightly tidied up, it can be officially opened to traffic. From now on, the products of Poyang Lake can be directly transported to Xunyang via Xingzi, and from Xun to Guling, it can also be transferred via Xingzi. In addition, Xiushui (ie, Yining Prefecture) to Pingjiang is a trunk line bordering Jiangxi and Hunan. After the leader of the 149th Brigade of the 50th Division, Wen Xiuxin, was appointed as the head of the Xiuping Highway Construction Department last winter, the construction started in November. After eight months, it has now been completed and the opening ceremony was held in Xiu on the 5th of this month, (15th)

Songjiang

Bandit Gang Sacks Ruanxiang Town 110

According to the report from Li Dengling, the head of the security detachment stationed in Shanyang, to the headquarters of the county's security team, at about 7 pm on the 19th, more than 50 bandits armed with guns attacked Ruanxiang, 12 miles away from Shanyang, speaking in a mixture of local dialects, and robbed each household in the whole town, lasting for about two hours. The bandits then dispersed and fled. There is no detailed report on the losses yet. According to reports, Ruanxiang is 12 miles away from Shanyang Jiangzhuang. Both Shanyang and Jiangzhuang have security teams stationed. After receiving the report, they led their teams to go, but the bandits had already fled far away.

Social Education Committee Established 111

The county party department followed the provincial order to organize a social education committee, which was presided over and convened by party committee members Xu Zhao and Wu Jiaju.
