Suzhou

Xukou Dam Construction Suspended 112

The dam built by the Construction Department in conjunction with the County Bureau in Xukou, Mudu, although the materials had been shipped there the day before, has now been suspended because the Hongshan Dam in Wuxi has been opened, and there is enough water in the river ports in various places, so the construction has been suspended and has not started. As for the small dam built by the villagers of Lingbang in Xukou, since there is already water in the bang, they no longer go to the dam to step on the waterwheel, but carry the waterwheel back to the fields to draw water.

Continuous Rainfall in the Four Townships 113

The sky in Suzhou was overcast from the morning of the 21st. Until about 8:00, there was a heavy rain again, and it did not stop until late at night. The rice seedlings were revitalized, and the wells and rivers rose, and the people were thankful to each other.

A Large Number of Workers Injured by Electric Shock 114

In the Shuyuan Lane area of the city, the telephone bureau sent craftsmen to replace cables on the 20th. Because a certain surname's electric light outside line in Sanduo Lane was damaged and touched the cable, all the mechanics and workers were electrocuted and fell to the ground. Among them, four mechanics were spared because they wore galoshes. They urgently used wooden sticks and other insulating equipment to rescue them. As a result, in addition to a worker named Jiang Xiaoheshang who died on the spot due to serious injuries, 15 people were injured, including mechanics Chen Meiqing, Liu Xiaochun, Xu Zhongkang, Yang Songqiao, Liu Zhenwu, Zhu Hengsheng, Zhou Zhensheng, Xiang Yongtang, Han Xuegao, Lu Xingqing, Zhao Shifa, Zhu Jingu, Zhou Lilin, Xu Ronggui, Shi Shunfa, and Wang Jinhua. Seven hired workers, including Lu Bingsheng, Zhou Ruxing, Huang Genbao, Pan Shusong, Wang Changsheng, Zhu Bingsheng, and Ji Wansheng, were all sent to Shende Hospital on Wusan Road for treatment. Yesterday (21st), they have all been discharged from the hospital one after another. Jiangyin

Wife Murderer Sentenced to Ten Years in Prison 115

At the Pinxiang Tea House in Zhangjie Alley, North Outer Street, Yao Dingjin, the brother-in-law of Zhao Ziyun from Yancheng, was a shop assistant in a noodle shop. At about 8:00 am on June 6th, he had a quarrel with his wife, Chen Erbao, and then killed his wife with a noodle knife. The murderer Yao Dingjin was sent to the county and sentenced yesterday (19th). Yao Dingjin's deliberate homicide was sentenced to ten years in prison and sent to the High Court for review and execution.

Weather Turns Cool, Showers Occasionally Fall 116

Recently, the weather has changed, the heatwave has subsided, and the mornings and evenings are just like early autumn. On the 18th and 19th, there were occasional showers in both urban and rural areas. Although not a heavy downpour, the bean and cotton crops have been nourished. Farmers still hope for more rain to ensure a good autumn harvest.

Wuxi

Strange News of Snowfall in July 117

Snowfall has a fixed time, being auspicious in winter and ominous in spring, but rarely occurring in May or June. On the 20th, around 10 AM, a strong wind blew through the Daxu Lane area of the Fourth District, with dark clouds gathering. A gust of wind even brought snowflakes, which melted upon landing, lasting for about three to four minutes. In Anzhen, the Seventh District, there was also snowfall after rain around 8 AM on the same day, stopping shortly after. The villagers were amazed. It is recalled that in late May of the 19th year of the Republic [1930], there was heavy snowfall in Dongzhou, at the border of Wuxi and Changzhou, which damaged fields and mulberry leaves. In June of the same year, there was also heavy snowfall in Baotou, devastating crops. Although there was light snowfall in Wuxi this time, the crops were not damaged.

Discussing the Treasury System for Deposit Management 118

The Wuxi County Government previously received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to implement the treasury system immediately. Local donations must be collected uniformly, and the order was followed accordingly. Yesterday, County Magistrate Yan convened an ad hoc political affairs meeting to discuss the conclusion of the 22nd year. Chen Yuchu, Shen Xichun, Hu Pinfang, Zang You, Zhang Fulin, Yu Tanfen, Qian Sunqing, Chen Zhanru, Xi Yaosun, Ye Dezhen, Gu Fengmao, Fei Yunong, Wu Shimei and others were present. Magistrate Yan reported on the order to implement the treasury system, requiring that funds from the 22nd year be kept in a special account and deposited in a treasury bank. After discussion, it was decided that civil affairs and education funds would be deposited in the Bank of Communications, industry funds in the Farmers Bank, and construction funds in the China-Jiangsu Bank, due to the history and interest rates of each institution. The amount to be allocated to the treasury included 20,000 yuan for civil affairs, 1,500 yuan for construction, 20,000 yuan for education, and 800 yuan for industry. The treasury seal must use the seals of the county magistrate, the chief accountant, and the director of the property department. Various new-style account books used by various institutions can be purchased directly from Xicheng Company. Statements should be submitted to the chief accountant for review by the 15th of each month. At the same time, the Finance Department also sent Commissioner Wang Maoqing to Wuxi to investigate the treasury system.

Zhenjiang

Representatives from Various Provinces Arrive in Jiangsu to Study Land Administration 119

Jiangsu Province pioneered land administration, taking the lead nationwide. Through diligent management, it has achieved considerable scale. Recently, the province's land administration work has become increasingly intensive, and the progress of the work has been particularly effective, attracting attention and importance from all parties. Representatives from various provincial governments are arriving in Jiangsu to study the matter in an endless stream. It is reported that Kong Lingcan, Shen Zhiqun, Li Bingrong, Cao Liqing, and Ou Benpeng from the Shandong Provincial Government; Chu Han and Xiong Daorui from the Hubei Provincial Department of Civil Affairs; He Shaoqiong, Liang Zishi, Liang Bangyan, and Lou Zhaoli from the Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance; Qi Wan from the Anhui Provincial Land Consolidation Office; Wen Renwu and Zhang Pengyi from the Hunan Provincial Department of Finance; and Qiu Yuyuan from the Fujian Provincial Department of Civil Affairs have all arrived. The Jiangsu Provincial Land Bureau has been sending representatives to provide sincere hospitality, explaining the implementation of various land administration tasks in Jiangsu, guiding them to visit various land administration facilities, and distributing various regulations and charts. The representatives from various provinces have expressed great satisfaction.

Fengxian

Ruanxiang Town Robbed by Bandits 120

Ruanxiang Town in our county was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits speaking the local dialect around 6 PM yesterday (the 19th). They carried two rifles and charged in from East Street, first seizing weapons from the public security police station before starting to rob. Most shops were closed and resisted. Only the Qiancaizhang and Tongshoutang businesses, and a Tang family resident, who was a woman and was eager to hide and didn't have time to close the door, were robbed by the bandits, who took a large amount of cash and jewelry. After looting, the bandits went to Qiancaizhang to exchange for 13 new straw hats, and a fat-faced bandit wearing a willow-striped short shirt and black pants called for the team to head towards the Jiutu area in the southeast. When the bandits surrounded the police station, patrol captain Zhang Yunbiao, seeing the urgency, jumped over the wall and fled to Zhuangxing Branch to report. At the same time, a Zhang family resident in the town secretly went to the Songjiang Jiangzhuang Town police station, about six li away from the town, to call for assistance. Troops arrived one after another that night, but the bandits were gone. It is now estimated that the total loss in the town is over 5,000 yuan. In addition to sending Qian, the section chief of the Public Security Bureau, to lead the police to investigate this afternoon (the 20th), the county government has also issued a general order to all police forces on land and water to arrest and bring the perpetrators to justice within ten days.

Gaoyou

Sweet Rain After a Long Drought 121

Our county has been suffering from a long drought, and the crops in the countryside have mostly withered. Today (the 19th) at 3 PM, dark clouds gathered in the sky, and sweet rain fell for a while, not stopping until late at night. An inch or so of rain has fallen, and the crops have benefited greatly. The general farmers are all overjoyed.

Nantong

Direct Connection of Nantong-Shanghai Telegram Line 122

Telegrams from Nantong to Shanghai were previously relayed through the Yang-Zhen water line, which caused delays when business telegrams were congested or military events occurred. The Ministry of Communications has now specially installed a direct Nantong-Shanghai line. The water line has been installed between Jiangyin and Jingjiang. This section of the water line has ten wires, three of which are long-distance telephone lines, one is for the Nantong-Shanghai water line, and the rest are for use by counties north of the Yangtze to communicate with the south.

Xiaoshan

Farmers Delighted by Sweet Rain After Long Drought 124

Xiaoshan had not rained for a long time, and people were panicking. Local gentry and merchants, for the sake of stabilizing people's hearts, set up altars in the Jiang Temple to pray for rain, and fasted for three days, and observed a seven-day abstinence from slaughter and performed repentance ceremonies. However, there was still no sign of rain. Starting on the 17th, Magistrate Zhang continued to ban slaughter for three days by order of the province, and all shrimp and fish were not allowed to be sold on the streets. Suddenly, on the morning of the 19th, an east wind blew strongly, and dark clouds covered the sun. At about 9 o'clock, heavy rain poured down, and the fields were filled with three inches of water in two hours. The farmers were overjoyed, and the weather turned cool. According to a survey, the planted crops throughout the county have been adequately watered. The unplanted fields are preparing for a second rain to replant.

Shaoxing

Rain Has Fallen, But Drought Has Not Receded 125

Shaoxing has been dry and rainless since the beginning of summer, and the heat has been exceptionally severe. The rice crops in the countryside have withered, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. A disaster is already forming. Farmers have set up altars to pray for rain, and the government has banned slaughter, hoping for rain. Everyone is anxiously waiting. After a drizzle fell the day before, the weather turned cooler. By the morning of the 19th, dark clouds gathered, and heavy rain poured down, stopping after about ten minutes, and the scorching sun returned. Although the heat has subsided, the drought has not receded. The water pump installed at Nanmentou was completed yesterday and can discharge water. In three to five days, there should be no shortage of water in the city's rivers. The county government has ordered that slaughter be banned for another three days starting from the 20th, by order of the province.

Ningbo

Rain Falls in Various Places, Weather Turns Cool 126

(1) It rained in this port around 4 AM on the 19th, and it has been sunny and rainy ever since, but it is all drizzle, and little water has been obtained. It is still lacking. Fortunately, the weather has suddenly turned cool, and the temperature has dropped to 81 or 82 degrees Fahrenheit, so the general coolies are happily relieved. (2) In Zhenhai Chongqiu Township and other places, there was heavy rain at 1 PM on the 18th, which lasted for half an hour. The water accumulated in the fields was more than half an inch. According to old farmers, fields closer to the river should have a 70% harvest after this rain. (3) In Cixi and other places, rain fell at 6 AM on the 19th, stopping after 15 minutes. At 10:50 AM, heavy rain poured down, lasting for about 20 minutes. After this soaking, the crops have benefited greatly.

Hangzhou

Rain on Farmland, Autumn Harvest Looks Promising 127

Hangzhou City has been dry and rainless since the beginning of summer, and the rivers have dried up. The farmland in the suburbs is cracked due to lack of irrigation. Farmers have rushed to the city government to report the emergency. Drinking water has become a problem in parts of the city without running water. Epidemics are especially rampant. The city government borrowed pumps and motors from power plants and installed them at the Lake Jian Great King Temple to draw water from the canal into the inner river, and opened the West Lake water gate to help irrigate farmland. Citizens set up altars in places such as Chenghuang Mountain to pray for rain, and the city government approved a six-day ban on slaughter. On the afternoon of the 18th, there was a first shower, but the scorching sun remained. On the 19th and 20th, there were successive showers. Yesterday (the 21st), the weather was like yellow fog, with showers in the morning, followed by drizzle. There was another shower at 1 PM. The farmland around the city has gained about three to five inches of water, and the crops have recovered. The farmers are quite happy, and the autumn harvest looks promising. The temperature has dropped to 84 degrees Fahrenheit, like early autumn. The epidemic atmosphere in the city has been greatly reduced.

Sudden Fire in Two Halls of the Prefectural Temple 128

At about 11 PM last night (the 20th), a fire suddenly broke out in the two halls of the Prefectural Temple in this city, and the flames soared into the sky. The Yilong firefighters from each district rushed to put out the fire. After about an hour of burning, it was extinguished. There are various rumors about the cause of the fire. According to the firefighters, the flames contained the smell of kerosene when they rose. It is now heard that several arson suspects have been arrested and taken to the County Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Local News

Yin Tong Left for Dalian Yesterday Morning 129

To meet with the Japanese Kwantung Army authorities to exchange views on whether or not Huang Fu will go north depending on the outcome of this trip. The issue of the North China War Zone will be the focus of discussion. Yin Tong, director of the Beining Railway Bureau, went south last time to meet with Wang Jingwei, the president of the Executive Yuan, and then went to Mogan Mountain to report the progress to Huang Fu. He came to Shanghai a few days ago and discussed again with Tang Yuren, the deputy minister of foreign affairs, and others. At 11 AM yesterday morning, Yin took the Japanese ship Dalian Maru to Dalian. He will meet with the Japanese Kwantung Army authorities in a private capacity to exchange important opinions on various issues in the North China War Zone. Whether or not Huang Fu will go north will depend on the outcome of Yin's trip. Details are listed below.

Left for Dalian Yesterday Morning 130

Yin Tong, director of the Beining Railway Bureau, and two attendants took a car directly to the Huangpu Wharf at around 9 AM yesterday morning and boarded the Japanese ship Dalian Maru. They booked a first-class room at the stern of the second floor and stayed inside with the door closed. He was extremely secretive beforehand, so there were few people seeing him off. The passenger list used a pseudonym such as Yu Wang. The reporter boarded the ship to look for him, but initially found nothing. It was not until five minutes before the ship was about to set sail that Yin stepped out onto the first-class deck and looked over the railing. The ship had already cast off its moorings when the reporter caught sight of him and hurriedly called out "Director Yin" from the dock. Yin nodded and smiled, but still pretended that he was going to Qingdao and not Dalian. The ship is scheduled to arrive in Dalian tomorrow morning.

The Mission of This Trip 131

Yin's trip to Dalian was decided after meeting Huang Fu on Mogan Mountain. Although the North China War Zone has been recovered, all the aftermath is manipulated by bandits and vagrants, making it impossible to handle. The Japanese side is making endless demands and using the war zone as a buffer zone to blackmail us. The North China authorities feel this is the most difficult thing to deal with. Huang Fu is passive, and this is the main reason. Therefore, Yin's trip is intended to meet with the Japanese Kwantung Army authorities in a private capacity, clearly explain the crux of the war zone issue, and inquire whether they are sincere.

Abolishing the Tanggu Truce 132

If they are, how should they be responsible for suppressing bandits and vagrants in the war zone, and how should they strictly stop all other acts of forcible occupation in accordance with legal principles? Otherwise, the negotiations will end there. Abolishing the Tanggu Truce is the second step. It will be handled by Huang Fu after Yin has negotiated a result, and then reported to the Central Government for approval.

Four Main Issues 133

Among the various issues in North China, the main ones, according to a certain important person yesterday, are roughly four items: (1) the reorganization of the security team of Li Jichun's old troops, (2) the withdrawal of the remaining Japanese troops at various passes of the Great Wall, (3) the roads built by Japan, and (4) the cancellation of the ceasefire agreement. Among these four important issues, the first two are the most urgent. Regarding the first item, the security team issue is related to the security of the entire war zone. The entire security team consists of 9,000 people, of which 5,000 are good people, and the remaining 4,000 are completely reorganized from Li Jichun's old troops. This security team not only does not abide by the rules and fulfill its security duties, but instead is protected by the Japanese and commits all kinds of evil. The remaining 5,000 good security team members have to guard these bad security team members. Therefore, all 9,000 security team members in the war zone are almost unusable, and security cannot be maintained. Therefore, the authorities intend to reorganize and train the 4,000 security team members of Li Jichun's old troops so that they all become useful teams. As for the second item, if Japanese soldiers who have not withdrawn from places such as Donglu and Malanyu, we cannot exercise administrative power, and Japanese vagrants and traitors collude, set up smoke and gambling dens everywhere, disrupt local security, and do everything they can. Therefore, these two items are urgent issues to be resolved.

Qixia Station on the Jinghu Railway

Suddenly Robbed Yesterday Morning 134

Guo, Xue, and Xu, the three stationmasters, were all beaten and injured. At 0:30 yesterday morning, a shocking incident occurred at Qixia Mountain Station on the Jinghu Railway, where the station was robbed and the stationmaster was beaten. The details are listed below.

Bandits Robbed 135

At 0:30 yesterday morning, fully armed bandits suddenly broke into the office of Qixia Mountain Station on the Jinghu Railway, as well as the station staff's quarters and the home of Xu Kechang, the stationmaster on duty, and looted all public and private property. They also beat and injured stationmasters Guo Changchun, Xue Boyin, and Xu Kechang. Ticket seller Zhang Wennuan was seriously injured. In the end, it is estimated that about 600 or 700 yuan of public and private property was lost, including only 33 yuan, 3 jiao, and 9 fen of station funds. The bandits then fled with the money.

Stationmaster Escaped 136

After robbing, the bandits also tied up Guo Changchun, the stationmaster on night duty. Fortunately, he managed to escape not far from the station and bravely returned. At that time, the 301st through train from Shanghai to Pingyang happened to arrive at the station. Stationmaster Guo immediately jumped onto the locomotive, guided the driver, and drove straight to Longtan to report the incident to the Longtan stationmaster.

Post-Incident Dispatch 137

After receiving the report, the Longtan stationmaster first dispatched the 301st through train at 1:20 this morning, delaying it by 31 minutes. He then used the dispatch telephone to report the details to the dispatching section of the traffic department. The section notified the resident railway police station and the traffic section chief of the Jingdan section, and ordered the Yao Huamen and Longtan stations to notify their respective railway protection troops to try to hunt down the bandits. Also, since the Qixia Mountain stationmasters were all injured and unable to work, the Yao Huamen station was ordered to dispatch a stationmaster to take the 503rd freight train with the railway protection troops to the Qixia station to temporarily maintain station operations.

Bureau's Actions 138

After receiving the news, Huang Boqiao, the director of the railway, ordered Xiao Weiguo, the chief of the traffic department, to go to the Qixia station with Ma Shaoping, the director of the resident railway police station, for a detailed inspection. He also telegraphed the Ministry of Railways, and also sent telegrams to the Capital Garrison Headquarters and the Nanjing Railway Police Administration Bureau. After receiving the report, Yang Xiaozeng, the traffic section chief of the Jingdan section of the railway, also rushed to the Qixia station from Nanjing this morning with a resident doctor to investigate, and the supplementary corps of the garrison dispatched a team to hunt down the bandits.

Last night

Hurricane Closer to Shanghai 139

Customs Has No Emergency Warnings, Shipping Routes South Closed, North Open, Huangpu River Evening Lighters All Stop. The hurricane warning signal is still flying high on the clock tower of the Jianghai Customs, but it is still a black ball and a red light, not the black cross and two red lights. Most of the ships from the Fujian and Zhejiang coasts to Shanghai are sheltering along the way, and the Shanghai-Ningbo liners have also been suspended. The China Merchants Putuo special service has also stopped running. Further details are listed below.

Hurricane Direction 140

According to the report of the Observatory, the direction of the hurricane from the Strait of Luzon and Taiwan has become north-northwest. The coast of Fuzhou will be spared, and the wind has blown to the Zhejiang waters, such as Wenzhou and Zhenhai. It is reported that the hurricane will not hit the coast of Wenzhou, with five winds blowing, and will be smaller in Zhenhai with three winds. The hurricane circle is 60 nautical miles around. Yesterday morning, the wind reached 120 degrees east longitude and 28 degrees north latitude. If it still moves north-northwest, Shanghai will inevitably be attacked. It is expected that the hurricane will reach Shanghai at 6 or 7 PM. But if it has not arrived at that time, the wind may have changed its direction. The Greater American Evening News said that, according to the Xujiahui Observatory, at 6 AM this morning (the 21st), the hurricane was about to 28.30 degrees north latitude and 120 degrees east longitude, moving to the northwest. If the direction does not change, it will pass west of Shanghai tonight. Its speed is still the same as between 6 PM last night and 6 AM this morning. According to the position reported by the Observatory, the hurricane should have entered the mountains of Zhejiang Province at 6 AM this morning, only about 160 miles from Shanghai. If it veers slightly east from now on, its full force may hit Shanghai. However, since this kind of storm is unpredictable, according to the opinion of meteorological experts, it may not reach Shanghai at all, or it may pass in a wide circle outside the border here and head for the Yellow Sea, which is difficult to predict.

Warning Navigation 141

Jianghai Customs has been flying a black ball on the top of the Great Bell Tower since 5 PM the night before, warning that the weather is bad and a hurricane is coming. At the same time, it is preparing a black cross mark for when the hurricane blows as a warning of the wind attack. Later, because there was no emergency notice from the Observatory that it would invade Shanghai immediately, it still flew a black ball yesterday. In the evening, a red light was added below the ball. If the wind arrives, two red lights must be hung. The Jianghai Customs warning cannon has not been fired because the time of the hurricane's arrival in Shanghai is not known for certain, so the black cross, two red lights, and the cannon have not been fired.

Pu'an Suspends Service 142

The China Merchants Pu'an ship was originally scheduled to sail to Putuo yesterday, and all tickets had been sold in advance. However, the Observatory's warning was received that the hurricane was the strongest in the Zhejiang waters. In order to be cautious about navigation, the Bureau decided to suspend the Putuo service temporarily, informing the passengers to change to Qingdao on the 24th. Passengers who do not want to refund their tickets can extend their trip and take the original ship next Saturday.

Shanghai-Ningbo Ships Stop 143

Yesterday, the Shanghai-Ningbo liners leaving Shanghai were the China Merchants Xin Jiangtian and the Sanbei Ningxing ships, which were also going to Putuo. Most of the passengers had already boarded the ship, but because the Shanghai-Ningbo route was right in the path of the hurricane, and there was a danger of traveling, the voyages were temporarily suspended. If there is no wind today, the two ships will leave today. The new Beijing and Xin Ningshao ships in Ningbo also sent an urgent telegram to Ningbo from Taikoo Ningshao, ordering them to stop in Ningbo and not sail to ensure safety.

Various Ships Late 144

Several ships from Shantou, Xiamen, and Guangzhou to Shanghai have sheltered from the wind along the way and have not yet arrived. Ships entering from Fuzhou, such as Jing'an, Yong'an, and Jiesheng, did not enter the port yesterday, because they were all moored along the way to avoid the hurricane. Because the ships did not arrive, there was no South China liner service in Shanghai. As for the coastal liners and small steamers along the coast of Zhejiang, all services were suspended yesterday. As for the North Sea liners and Yangtze River export ships, they sailed as usual, but were prepared along the way to prevent the hurricane from changing direction. The ships moored outside the Wusong mouth are also waiting for the wind to advance or retreat to determine their course.

Huangpu River Prepared 145

Yesterday, the cargo barges, civil ships, and sculling boats in the Huangpu River were very strictly prepared, especially in the evening. After 6 PM, there were no sculling boats sailing on the Huangpu River, and most of them sailed into the old port to take shelter temporarily.

Five Days of Drizzle in This City 146

Heavier Rainfall Yesterday Morning

Crops Have Hope of Recovery Since the sweet rain fell on the 17th of this month, there have been continuous drizzles for a total of five days, until yesterday. The rain that fell yesterday morning was heavier. It had been raining off and on since late the night before, and yesterday morning, dark clouds suddenly gathered, and heavy rain poured down in an instant. Unfortunately, it was too short, stopping after 20 minutes. It drizzled again before long, and it stopped and rained until the evening. As a result, most of the summer heat has subsided, and the cool breeze is blowing. The farmers in the countryside are all overjoyed to get this sweet rain, and the crops have hope of recovery.

After Rain in This City

Autumn Harvest Can Be Expected Without Obstruction 147

Central News Agency reports that since the beginning of summer, this city has been suffering from drought, which has caused the general public to worry deeply about the lack of hope for the autumn harvest. The high price of rice has also caused unrest among the common people. The municipal government ordered the responsible agencies to suppress the price of rice and purchased water pump machines for farmers to pump water and irrigate their fields. Recently, because of the sweet rain, the crops have been able to recover, and people's hearts have been greatly stabilized. The price of rice has also shown a trend of falling. According to the news obtained by the reporter's investigation, it is listed below.

Rice Prices Gradually Fall 148

The reporter visited the rice industry yesterday and learned that since the sweet rain fell the day before, rice prices have become slightly looser, and the rice boats in various villages were scarce due to the low water level in the rivers. If it continues to rain and the river water is higher, rice transportation will be restored, and the price of rice is even more likely to fall. Therefore, the matter of purchasing foreign rice may be temporarily shelved. It is rumored that the Soviet Union will transport a large amount of rice to China. The rice industry in this city does not have this news. Since the Customs Bureau has collected taxes on foreign rice, the sales of rice such as Burmese rice have not been as strong as in previous years.

Continue to Pump Water 149

According to the person in charge of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the farmland in this city has withered due to the drought, and the municipal government purchased water pump machines and allocated them to various villages for use. The fire brigades in various districts used pump trucks to pump water to irrigate the fields, and the farmland benefited greatly. Recently, sweet rain has fallen again, and the crops have had the hope of recovery. If the weather turns sunny and hot again and the farmland still feels a lack of water, it can continue to pump water to irrigate the fields, so most of the autumn harvest in this city can be expected without obstruction.

Gu Xinyi Returned to Shanghai Yesterday 150

Stabilizing Rice Prices Results in Satisfaction Shenshi News Agency reports that Gu Xinyi, the leader of the rice industry, went to Beijing on the evening of the 17th to meet with President Wang, requesting measures to stabilize the rising price of rice and proposing to purchase 500,000 dan of tax-free imported foreign rice to suppress the price. Gu has now returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. The Shenshi News Agency reporter has learned that the Executive Yuan has fully accepted Gu's opinions and approved the issuance of a tax-free import license for foreign rice, which will be purchased and imported successively by the Civil Food Control Design Committee according to the needs of the market. It is expected that rice prices will be stabilized in the future and will not rise excessively again. In addition, the Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau, which is organized by eight provinces, has now been formally decided by the Executive Yuan to be managed by the Ministry of Finance. The shares that have been paid to each province will be refunded separately to end the matter. The Ministry of Finance has also found funds for the operating expenses of the Grain Transportation Bureau and will soon be able to organize and establish it.

Decision by the Military Council of the Executive Yuan

New Measures for Sending Northeastern Army Dependents 152

Taking the route through Suiyuan and Ningxia to Xinjiang, travel expenses of 100,000 are allocated by the Ministry of Finance. The dependents of officers and soldiers of the Northeastern armies under Li Du, Su Bingwen, Wang Delin, etc., who retreated to Russian territory after the anti-Japanese war and then transferred to Xinjiang, entered the country through Vladivostok and scattered in various places such as Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, reaching hundreds of people. Except for those who stayed in place and were given severance pay to return to their hometowns, 131 of them need to be sent to Xinjiang to reunite their families. General Li Du, former Deputy Commander of the Northeastern Border Defense Army stationed in Jilin, petitioned Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission with measures. Now, the Executive Yuan Military Affairs Commission has decided to take the route through Suiyuan and Ningxia to Xinjiang. The journey will start soon, with travel expenses of 100,000 allocated by the Ministry of Finance. The contents of the measures are as follows:

Preparation for Sending and Route 153

After the Military Affairs Commission decided on the measures for sending the Northeastern Army dependents to Xinjiang, it sent a letter to the Executive Yuan, which was handed over to the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ministry of Finance for review. The First Department of the Military Commission sent a letter to General Li Du, with the original text of the measures as follows: Measures for sending, (1) Preparation for sending, (A) Regarding the dependents of Jilin military officers stationed in Xinjiang who are currently living in Shanghai, Tianjin, and Beijing, Commander Li Du should first conduct separate investigations and inquire whether they are willing to go to Xinjiang, as well as their parents' current positions and stationed locations, and prepare a clear list for verification. (B) After the above investigation is clarified, Commander Li Du will appoint escorts and prepare a preliminary schedule for gathering the dependents in Shanghai, Tianjin, and Beijing. He will consult with the Ministry of Military Affairs to determine the departure time and notify the dependents to board the train on time. (C) All dependents willing to go to Xinjiang should be notified to prepare themselves in advance so that they can depart at any time. (2) Route for sending. It is decided to enter Xinjiang through Suiyuan and Ningxia, divided into three sections for transportation, as specified below. (A) From Shanghai via Tianjin and Beijing to Baotou is the first section. The railway department is requested to order all routes to prepare trains for transportation. (B) From Baotou to Ningxia is the second section. The Suiyuan Provincial Government will provide transportation by car. (C) From Ningxia to Dihua is the third section. The Ningxia Provincial Government will continue to use cars for transportation.

Ministry of Finance Allocates Travel Expenses 154

(3) Funds for sending should be listed in a special budget estimate, and temporary advance payment methods should be provisionally proposed. (A) Subsistence: From the day of boarding the train, each dependent will be issued a subsistence allowance of four dimes (0.4 yuan) of silver per day. For the first section of the journey, Commander Li Du will prepare a budget, receive it and hand it over to the escorts for management and distribution, and report it after completion. For the second section of the journey, the Suiyuan and Ningxia provincial governments will check the number of dependents, estimate the transportation date for this section, and verify and advance the payment. (B) Car expenses: The expenses for cars used in the second and third sections will be paid in advance by the Suiyuan and Ningxia provincial governments and reported together for verification and reimbursement afterward. (C) The aforementioned expenses will be issued by the Ministry of Finance and a summary estimate will be made for special expenditure. (4) Others, (A) When the dependents are sent off on their journey, a telegram will be sent to the Xinjiang Provincial Government immediately to notify the parents to prepare for resettlement in advance. (B) During the three legs of the journey from Baotou via Ningxia to Dihua, the Ministry of Military Affairs will, upon the start of the dispatch, notify the troops stationed along the way to protect them properly.

Letter from the Executive Yuan to Li Du 155

Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, also ordered Secretary-General Chu Minyi to send a letter to General Li Du, the original text of which reads: "Following the instruction of President Wang, the case was checked and the official letter from the Military Affairs Commission regarding the five post-war measures proposed by Li Du, Deputy Commander of the Northeastern Border Defense Army stationed in Jilin, was previously approved. Among them, regarding the third item, requesting funds for sending dependents to Xinjiang, it was forwarded for verification and handling. Subsequently, a letter was approved and sent to the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ministry of Finance, jointly formulating measures, and a letter was sent to the Military Affairs Commission in reply, stating that the situation in Xinjiang has recently been unclear. According to telegrams from Consul Xu in Boli (Khabarovsk) and Sheng Shicai, it seems that the internal organization of Li Du's troops has been reorganized. It would be very inconvenient for these women and children to travel thousands of miles. If the dependents are willing to go to Xinjiang, the central government may provide travel expenses for them to go on their own. Please verify and instruct them to comply, etc. In addition to ordering the Ministry of Military Affairs to forward the instructions for compliance and informing the Ministry of Finance, the Secretariat should record the case and forward it to the original petitioner, etc. A complete copy of the case is enclosed for your information. This is addressed to Li Du, Deputy Commander of the Northeastern Border Defense Army stationed in Jilin. Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan."

Current Situation of Various Armies Stationed in Xinjiang 156

More than 10,000 soldiers of the Northeastern armies under Li Du, Su Bingwen, Wang Delin, etc., who retreated to Russia and went to Xinjiang, still used the army numbers from when they were in Jilin and Heilongjiang. According to Wang Ziyao, adjutant of General Li, recently, personnel from the army departed from Xinjiang and walked for more than 50 days, experiencing many hardships along the way. They arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and reported the current situation of the stationed troops to Generals Li and Wang in Shanghai. He learned that the Northeastern Army in Xinjiang suffered a quarter of casualties during the two political changes in Xinjiang last winter when Dihua was besieged by Ma Zhongying's troops, leaving more than 8,000 people. They have now withdrawn from Dihua, the capital of Xinjiang, and are stationed in seven counties including Ili, Tacheng, Suilai, Usu, Hami, Turpan, and Yanqi. The cost of living is meager, and they are very distressed. They hope that the central military authorities will reorganize them and grant them official status. The local situation in Xinjiang is relatively stable. Zhang Peiyuan, the Border Defense Commissioner of Xinjiang, indeed committed suicide in Ili last November. Ma Zhongying failed to besiege Dihua and retreated to Kashi, southern Xinjiang. He had not heard of the retreat to Russia. Xinjiang is adjacent to Soviet Russia, and the military and commercial influence of Soviet Russia in Xinjiang is very alarming. The Soviet Union has built a railway in Xinjiang (Turkestan-Siberia Railway), which has been completed. The Chinese people should not ignore the issues of national defense and diplomacy in this remote western Xinjiang.

Yu Youren Denies Resignation 158

"A time of national crisis is not the time for us to leave," said Xin Sheng News Agency. Yesterday, foreign newspapers reported that Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, had resigned. Yesterday morning, Yu's aides formally denied the report, saying that the resignation rumor was purely due to a misunderstanding caused by the lack of unified language in China. On the morning of the 19th of this month, three reporters visited Yu at the same time. At that time, he happened to want to dispel rumors from outside, so he briefly expressed his recent thoughts. Unexpectedly, due to language issues, a misunderstanding arose. At that time, Yu believed that being an official was not as pleasant as being a commoner. If he were a commoner, he could of course enjoy a leisurely life in the countryside. However, now that he is serving the country and at a time of national crisis, no one can easily shirk his responsibilities for any reason. Therefore, Yu has consistently refused to express any opinion on the twists and turns of this impeachment case by the Control Yuan. This is probably also to consider the future of the country. In short, Yu's words are indeed passive, but he believes that the country is currently in a difficult situation, and it is not the time for people like him to leave, so he has not taken any actual action to resign.

British American Tobacco Company

After the Labor Dispute is Resolved 160

The worker maintenance team is scheduled to withdraw this morning.

According to Da Gong News Agency, the British American Tobacco factory shutdown dispute has been resolved by the party and government organs through six agreed-upon measures, which have been ordered to be followed by both the union and the company. After receiving the instructions, the Strike Committee immediately convened a temporary meeting for discussion and unanimously agreed to comply. However, there were still one or two minor details regarding the follow-up matters after the resumption of work that needed to be referred to the Municipal Party Committee. Therefore, several representatives, including Liu Dehua and Zhang Ziping, were dispatched to the Municipal Party Committee for instructions yesterday morning. Committee Member Wu Kaixian received them, and after Committee Member Wu explained in detail, the results of the negotiation were quite satisfactory. After reporting back to the committee, a notice was issued, notifying the workers of the resumption of work arrangements. The Da Gong News Agency reporter also crossed the Huangpu River to visit Party Committee Member Chen Junyi. According to Chen, the British American Tobacco factory shutdown dispute has lasted for two months. After repeated mediation by party and government organs, as well as the assistance of community leaders such as Du Yuesheng and the General Labor Union, six resolution measures have now been decided and instructed to both parties. The workers have clearly understood the overall situation and have expressed their compliance. Work can definitely resume next Monday (tomorrow), and all maintenance teams can also withdraw tomorrow morning (i.e., today). Regarding the issuance of relief funds to the new factory workers during the strike period, the authorities are paying close attention to handling it seriously. It is expected to be cleared in the next two days, Saturday and Sunday. At that time, the municipal government, the municipal party committee, and the Social Affairs Bureau will jointly send personnel to handle it. For prudence, the issuance will be based on union registration certificates, factory badges, and other credentials that can prove that they are new factory workers (because some do not have badges). Chiefs and staff from various workshops will also be invited to the venue to verify to avoid fraudulent claims. Chen also said that he had been ordered by the Municipal Party Committee to come to Pudong to persuade the workers for many days, and he felt quite exhausted in spirit. Fortunately, the labor dispute is about to end, and the order during the strike period was good, and no incidents occurred, which is deeply gratifying. He earnestly hoped that both labor and management would not cause more trouble in the future, so that both parties would benefit. It was also learned that after the union maintenance team withdraws this morning, the order at the factory gate will be maintained by the Public Security Bureau dispatching police. Also, fearing that unscrupulous individuals might go to the union to cause trouble, the Public Security Bureau has also dispatched police to the union to protect it since yesterday afternoon.

Inland Rivers of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Provinces

Unanimously Oppose Inspection by the Ministry of Communications 165

Presented to Minister Zhu for temporary suspension of implementation of ship and crew regulations. Since the Ministry of Communications announced the regulations for the inspection of inland river ship crews, the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui have unanimously opposed it. Industry associations from the three provinces have appointed the industry associations in Nanjing and Shanghai to draft a request to abolish the inspection of crew members on ships under 50 tons, and to postpone the inspection date for those over 50 tons. The joint presentation is excerpted as follows: "Presented to request a temporary suspension of the implementation of the provisional regulations on the inspection of crew members for vessels navigating inland rivers over 50 gross tons, in order to maintain inland river navigation and protect the livelihoods of existing crew members. It is respectfully reported that the tonnage of all vessels of our member bureaus is mostly between 20 tons and 50 gross tons. This time, your ministry has promulgated and implemented the provisional regulations on the inspection of crew members for vessels under 50 gross tons, which not only fail to meet the actual requirements of inland river ship crew members in performing their duties but also provide no benefit to the safety and security of our inland river shipping businesses. In addition to stating the current situation and requesting abolition in a separate document, it is found that some member bureaus have vessels over 50 gross tons, and they all find the provisional regulations on the inspection of crew members difficult to comply with. The reason is that the above regulations may be applicable to crew members serving on the high seas, but the routes of the vessels over 50 gross tons of our member bureaus are all inland rivers. The scope is narrow, the dangers are few, and the service conditions of the crew members cannot be compared with those of high seas vessels. Moreover, the origins of the existing crew members are the same as those of the crew members of vessels between 20 gross tons and 50 gross tons. They all rise gradually and do not advance by jumping levels. They not only have considerable experience in navigation knowledge and practical skills, but also have a tacit understanding of the current routes. In terms of physical condition, they are all healthy, and in terms of service, they are all competent. Good and old skippers hold the power of the life of a ship. When the owners are in charge of employing people, how can they not pay attention to it? In the labor side, there is no way to get a job if you are incompetent. It is also difficult to blame the failure of navigation entirely on the lack of service. In short, inspecting crew members and focusing on practical skills are the most urgent tasks. You must not overemphasize literal meaning and neglect practical experience. If it is said that holding a piece of certificate can determine that they must be competent, it is difficult to believe deeply. I humbly believe that the law is nothing more than human sentiment. Our navigation authorities should, in this time of decline in inland river navigation and extreme difficulty in the lives of existing crew members, urgently maintain the status quo, so that the survival relationship between labor and management can also be maintained, and the hard work of our inland river merchants can be salvaged in the future. Our associations believe that this matter concerns the business of inland river merchants and the livelihoods of existing crew members, which is of utmost importance. We venture to submit this joint document, hoping that the authorities will grant approval and carefully examine and approve the temporary suspension of the implementation of the provisional regulations on the inspection of crew members for vessels navigating inland rivers over 50 gross tons in order to maintain inland river navigation and protect the livelihoods of existing crew members. With great urgency and anticipation, we respectfully present this to Zhu, Minister of Communications. Nanjing Shipping Association, (Chief drafter) Shanghai Inland River Ship Industry Association, Zhenjiang Shipping Association, Wuhu Small Ship Industry Association, Hangzhou Ship Industry Association, Wuxian Ship Association, Wuxi County Shipping Association, Wuxing County Ship Industry Association, Pinghu County Ship Industry Association, trade unions."

Special District Rickshaw Industry Association

Please Negotiate for the Abolition of the Vehicle Committee 171

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, since the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession established the Rickshaw Affairs Committee, all vehicle owners and rickshaw pullers have expressed their opposition to its impractical measures. Yesterday, the Special District Rickshaw Industry Association submitted petitions to the municipal government, the municipal party committee, the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Bureau of Social Affairs, requesting negotiations to abolish the organization of the committee. The original text reads: "Presented to request assistance in negotiating the use of concession rights to organize and implement forced oppression on more than 100,000 people in the rickshaw industry, leaving rickshaw pullers waiting to die. Since the industry began, it has been in operation for many years. There are more than 1,000 vehicle owners and more than 100,000 rickshaw pullers, all of whom are working day and night to support their lives. The tax responsibilities they bear are also quite heavy. The total amount of Chinese, British and French donations and license fees each year is more than 600,000 yuan. This kind of business can be said to be a great contribution to the propertyless poor. If not for the tolerance of our industry, society would have had a few more unemployed people. From this, it can be seen that the rickshaw industry is actually a profit-generating machine, and all government offices should protect it, how can they destroy it? How would we know the facts prove that it is just the opposite. Ever since the Zhabei Incident in 1932, Chinese and foreign businesses have been stagnated, and the various rickshaw industries have suffered the most due to traffic congestion, and have been almost unable to recover. Fortunately, the vehicle owners have worked hard to fight and maintain it in every possible way. In the current economic downturn, there is finally a glimmer of dawn and a slight sign of prosperity. Unexpectedly, this has agitated the jealousy of imperialism. In addition, unscrupulous elements have assisted and cheered from the sidelines, either wanting to take it over for public ownership or thinking about increasing taxes. Various strategies are nothing more than pleasing foreigners, but fearing that it would conflict with the Yangjingbang regulations, they cleverly created a name and established the Rickshaw Affairs Management Committee to manage rickshaw affairs. Since its establishment, the committee has been able to oppress vehicle merchants. Today, it is cracking down on vehicle parts and replacing vehicle shells. Tomorrow, it is registering rickshaw pullers and increasing monthly donations, breaking up vehicle merchant groups, and alienating both sides. Vehicle merchants cannot do business with peace of mind, and vehicle renters and rickshaw pullers are all in danger. The undercurrent of the market is frightening, and the atmosphere is extremely tense. Our industry has witnessed the situation and is deeply worried. If the committee is obsessed and does not wake up, it will inevitably create a special opportunity and be used by the Communist Party, and the future will be dire. Our department has repeatedly argued with reason, painfully stated the advantages and disadvantages, and issued declarations twice. We have also listed in detail the committee's unrealistic and inhumane suggestions, and have run around calling for help, with sore lips and dry tongues, but the committee has turned a deaf ear and continued to act arbitrarily. At present, the committee is becoming even more aggravated. It has summoned vehicle merchants for talks, and starting from August 1, it will increase the monthly donation by $1.50 per rickshaw as the committee's regular operating expenses and half as a mutual aid business. Finally, it issued a serious tone, saying that if vehicle merchants have any resistance, the committee will have its own ways to deal with it. At that time, it may ask the authorities to punish or reassign the vehicle license to a new car dealership. This kind of measure by the committee is simply insane and unreasonable. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt, the economy is collapsing, and disaster has struck both sides of the Yangtze River, many famine-stricken farmers from various counties have come to this port to pull rickshaws for food. In addition, the number of original rickshaw pullers is really shocking. At this time of trouble, those who hold this political power should be cautious, calm, and maintain the status quo in order to cope with the special crisis. Who knows that the committee is taking advantage of this extraordinary time to arbitrarily change the rules, overthrow the old cases, arouse outside doubts, and stir up the rickshaw industry trend. If there is any improper handling, it will inevitably lead to a great tragedy. At that time, at least it will harm the city's public security, and at worst, it will affect international negotiations. Our industry has seen and heard this, how can we be silent? We hereby state the whole process of the committee's extortion and the uneasy phenomenon of vehicle owners and rickshaw pullers, and appeal to your government, meeting, bureau and office for examination and approval. You must uphold justice, negotiate strictly, and send a letter to the British Municipal Council, immediately abolishing the illegal rickshaw affairs management committee and still being controlled by the former vehicle affairs office, so as to eliminate hidden dangers and secure livelihoods. We cannot help but to lead and wait for orders."

Yesterday's Discussion Meeting Convened

Three Key Points for Relief Decided

Since the beginning of summer this year, the weather has been severely dry, rivers and lakes have dried up, farmland has cracked, and rice crops have withered. The autumn harvest is unlikely, and a disaster is imminent, especially in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Now, Shaoxing sojourners in Shanghai, including Chen Jiufeng, concerned about their hometown, convened a discussion meeting at the 8th branch of the Municipal Federation at 2 PM yesterday. (2) Du Chunsu was asked to draft the constitution, to be discussed at the next meeting. (3) In addition to the original eleven founders, it is proposed to add Wang Yansong, He Wuliang, Fan Gaoping, Hu Yuzhi, Hu Zhongchi, Wei Jinshan, Feng Buqing, Qian Junren, Lu Yunsu, Yu Yeqing, and others as founders to strengthen the effort. (5) Three key points for relief were decided: (A) Drought relief, (B) Flood relief, (C) Relief for other disasters. Chinese National Wang Shijie

Invents Cost-Effective Electric Advertisement 181

Superior to Neon Glass Tubes

Chinese national Wang Shijie, who studied in Lyon, France, has returned to China. In view of the high price of the original neon electric glass tubes, he has invented the Jingxia electric advertisement to save electricity costs. The electrical device is installed inside a box, which can be large or small. (The installation method is patented and cannot be disclosed.) Reduced

School Chemistry Transportation Fees 182

The Railway Bureau previously considered that the railway transport of chemical products was mostly for school experiments, so the amount transported was at most a few pounds of each type, and there was rarely a large batch transport. It seemed that it could not be charged according to the second-class minimum freight rate. It was specially requested from the Ministry of Railways that chemical products with explosive or dangerous properties used by school laboratories should be allowed to change the provision that the minimum freight should be calculated according to the second-class rate, in order to negotiate the situation. Subsequently, the Ministry ordered (Industry Letter No. 25653) to allow new regulations. The freight for chemical products transported by formal schools may be calculated according to the minimum freight for less-than-carload freight, starting at 50 kilograms. The Railway Bureau is now announcing the implementation from July 1st. However, it is stipulated that in the future, if any station transports chemical products with dangerous properties, one of the consignors and consignees must be a formal school, and must provide a formal letter of certification from the school. This certificate letter should be submitted along with the freight ticket to the accounting office for verification, otherwise the second-class minimum fee will still be charged.

Injury and Death Verified 184

Landlord Delayed Repairs, Unfortunately Causing a Major Tragedy - At about 1 PM the day before yesterday, the houses at Nos. 158 and 156 North Fujian Road suddenly collapsed due to years of disrepair, killing two women on the spot and injuring six elderly and young people. Yesterday, it suddenly collapsed, etc. Wang Achang, a worker from Shaoxing, testified that he rented a house at No. 158 and that the deceased Wang Chen was his wife. He was working outside when the wall collapsed yesterday, so he did not know about it at the time. After obtaining the testimony, Zhang Jun ordered that the deceased Yuan Ma and Wang Chen were both killed by being crushed. Yuan Ma's body was handed over to Yuan Xiaoquan and Wang Chen's body was handed over to Wang Achang, who signed the certificates separately and took them back for burial.

The text of the memorial, which was changed to be submitted this morning due to the rain yesterday, is extracted as follows: "On July 21st of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, that is, the tenth day of the sixth month of the Jiaxu year in the Xiazheng calendar, Buddhist disciples Wang Zhen, Xu Guannan, Shao Ruxin, etc., after fasting and bathing, respectfully offer incense with utmost sincerity, and piously knock on the throne of the Jade Emperor, and Chen Ci Ri: 'The country takes the people as its foundation, and the people take food as their heaven. The Chinese people have long been covered and nurtured, and have been born together. I never thought that since the beginning of summer this year, the drought demon has wreaked havoc, and the rain master has lost his job, resulting in rivers drying up, farmland cracking, red land for thousands of miles, and heat increasing sharply. The autumn harvest is therefore hopeless, and epidemics are born from it. Since the great flood in various provinces in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the afflicted people have not been able to breathe steadily for three years amid internal troubles and foreign disasters. Now, they are suffering from drought, living in deep water and hot fire, and the lives of the people are like silk threads. Disasters are circulating, and there is no way to appeal. I think that heaven has the virtue of loving life, and Buddhism values the merit of saving the dead. Even the slightest of ants are cherished, and the violence of tigers and wolves is not punished. Therefore, we unite with the Buddhist and Taoist religions, philanthropists, and devout women, and pray sincerely to plead for the drought-stricken areas in various provinces and cities across the country. I respectfully ask the emperor to show his judgment, and pour down sweet rain to eliminate disasters, so that the people can live in peace and the country can be prosperous, the times can be harmonious, and the years can be abundant. I have laid bare my report and feel extremely frightened and worried.' Sincerely, the report."

Completion Today 189

The prayer for rain and disaster relief conference, which started with the issuance of talismans on the 20th, will be completed this afternoon (22nd). Celestial Master Zhang Ruiling has scheduled to burn talismans, retreat the gods, and descend from the altar at 5 PM this afternoon. The merits of praying will be completed by this time.

Death from Toothache by Mistakenly Taking Medicine Powder

Yang Xiao's Post-Mortem Examination Pending 190

Yang Fuhai Detained Pending Investigation - Yang Fuhai, a resident of Pudong Gaojia, his wife Yang Xiao suffered from severe toothache on the night of the 16th of this month. Yang Fuhai took the medicine powder and asked her to swallow it. (Yang is a Chinese medicine doctor and also practices surgery, so he has various medicines at home.) Unexpectedly, after taking the medicine, she shouted in pain, asking her husband if he had taken the wrong medicine powder, causing her intestines to feel like they were being cut with a knife. Yang also admitted that he might have taken the wrong medicine powder. He was at a loss and did not have time to treat her. Xiao died of exhaustion until dawn. The local defense corps detained Yang Fuhai and sent him to the Fourth District Police Station for interrogation, and reported to the local court to send someone to verify the truth. The body was sent to Zhenru for autopsy. Yesterday, Yang Fuhai was sent by the Fourth District Police Station to the Third Section and sent to the local court for interrogation. After the prosecutor's inquiry, he was ordered to be detained pending investigation.

On the Third-Floor Mezzanine

Fifteen Bags of Red Pills Seized 191

Suspicious Small Girl Named as Defendant Along With Woman - Detective Wang Chenying and Detective Wang Guangtian of the Jiaxing Road Police Station learned that someone was selling drugs for profit in the house at No. 37 Hongye Fang, Wuzhou Road. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, they cooperated with Chinese and foreign police to search the house. They saw local woman Chen Yao and others gathering to play mahjong there, but no red pills were found. Strangely, they later found out that the pills were hidden at No. 35 next door, on the third-floor mezzanine. They went to that building and copied 15 bags of red pills weighing 123 and a half taels. They asked the second landlord, Yong woman Zhu Caixiang, and learned that Chen Yao had rented the building and moved in on the 29th of last month. Only a small girl came to stay every night, and the rent was 4 yuan and a half per month, but she did not know that red pills were hidden. She lived in the front building of No. 37. The detectives went to check the front building and found a white crepe cloth, green buttoned shirt. Its size was no different from what Chen Yao was wearing. They arrested her and took her and the red pills to the police station. The head of the detectives ordered her to be sent to the women's prison. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Attorney Li Zhishan of the Public Works Bureau stated the previous situation and said that the defendant denied it at the police station. He now filed a public prosecution in accordance with Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law and requested a postponement for detailed investigation. He then presented the red pills and a shirt for inspection. Zhu Caixiang, the second landlord of No. 35, proved the process and pointed out that the girl who came to sleep every night was listening to the court. Attorney Li asked the detectives to put the girl in the witness box. She claimed to live upstairs at No. 350 Dayou Lane, Wuzhou Road. Her name was Wang Zhaodi, 15 years old, from Nanjing. She knew the defendant because she lived downstairs and I often went to a certain woman in the front building of No. 35 to hang out and watch her play mahjong. She did not know about the red pills hidden in the third-floor mezzanine, and had not stayed in that mezzanine. When asked of the defendant, she completely denied it, saying that she had lived with her mother at No. 250 Dayou Lane for many years since her husband died when she was 19 years old. The red pills copied from the mezzanine belonged to someone else. The rest of her testimony was evasive. Attorney Li asked to detain the girl Zhaodi and add her to the defendant's position, as the girl was highly suspicious. Judge Wu Zehan approved and ordered Wang Zhaodi to be temporarily detained to investigate and handle whether she was an accomplice. Chen Yao was taken back to prison and the hearing was rescheduled.

World's Fattest Woman Arrives in Shanghai 192

Waist Circumference Sixty-Four Inches

The Shanghai Times reported that Neli, the world's fattest woman, weighing over seven hundred pounds, arrived in Shanghai yesterday (20th) on the President Cleveland from Japan. When she landed at the New Customs Wharf at 9 AM, pedestrians stopped to watch. The woman is 26 years old and was born in Columbus, Ohio, USA. When she landed, she weighed only 5 pounds. At the age of 12, she weighed 85 pounds and continued to increase year by year. By the age of 18, she already weighed 616 pounds. Since then, she has joined various age groups and has traveled around the world five times. There is no one who doesn’t know her. Although the woman is fat, her appetite is the same as that of ordinary people, but she is very healthy and has never been ill for a day. Two years ago, a famous doctor in Los Angeles examined her body. Before the examination, he expected that she would not live to be 35 years old, but after the examination, he said that she could reach old age. In addition to doing gentle gymnastics every day, the woman walks for a short time. Her upper arm circumference is 26 inches, her knees are 36 inches, her thighs are 48 inches, and her waist circumference is 64 inches. However, her feet are only 5 and a half inches long, and her hands are not big either. This is the woman's first time arriving in Shanghai. She will perform at the Dahua Garden on Haig Road for a month.

Demon? He Shou Wu? - Jiang Gengfu, the 16-year-old son of Jiang Agen, a farmer in Xingtangwu, north of Minhang Town in the southwest of this city, went to cut grass near Longyin Temple the day before yesterday afternoon. Insufficient Rainfall

Inland River Steamer Schedules Not Yet Restored 199

However, the weather has turned cooler and melon crops have been greatly affected. Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the weather in this city has gradually become cooler since the rainfall, but the water volume is not large, so inland river steamers have not been able to operate as usual. Melon crops have been greatly reduced in price due to the cooler weather. Recently, the lower-level offices on the Huangpu Bund are concerned about typhoons hitting Shanghai and the possibility of the Huangpu River overflowing, and are carrying out defensive work. The following is a report from the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter after investigation:

Schedules Not Restored 200

The schedules of small steamers of the Inland River Steamer Bureau to Suzhou, Wuxi, Kunshan, Changshu, Hangzhou, Shengze, Huzhou, Xiashi, and other places have been suspended for a long time due to drought and water depletion on the Shanghai-Xiashi line and the Shanghai-Huzhou line. The Shanghai-Xiashi line now operates to Pinghu, and the Shanghai-Huzhou line operates to Nanxun. The remaining lines are temporarily maintained by ships with smaller tonnage. Although there has been rain recently, the water volume is too small and the time is too short, so the water level in the river has risen very little and is still not smooth. According to the China Merchants Inland River Steamer Bureau, if it rains for a few more days and the water level can rise by three to five inches, ships in various inland rivers can travel smoothly without obstruction and restore their schedules.

Melon Prices Depreciate 201

The weather was extremely hot a week ago. In this city, there was a general lack of watermelons and various melons in the markets. Therefore, the villagers from various places who came to Shanghai to sell melons early all left with good prices. Hearing that watermelons in Shanghai could be sold at good prices, farmers from various places transported them to Shanghai in large quantities by agreement. However, after arriving in Shanghai, it rained and the weather turned cooler. What could be sold for three or four yuan a load before is now only one yuan and two jiao per load, all of which are top-quality white watermelons and potato melons. Therefore, they are all dejected and lament their bad luck. The prices of various vegetables are also slightly cheaper than in the past.

Defensive Works 202

The weather has been cloudy and rainy recently. According to the report of the Observatory, there is a possibility of a typhoon hitting Shanghai. Yesterday, the water in the Huangpu River also rose greatly due to weather conditions. Those with lower-level offices along the Huangpu Bund Road, in view of the previous incident where the river water rushed onto the road due to a typhoon, causing the offices to be flooded and endangering various items, have hired workers to rush to build defenses in preparation, so as not to repeat the previous mistakes.

Pudong Qichang Warehouse

The Verdict in the Case of Stealing Electricity from the Yiji Meat Shop 208

Gu Gao, a local woman, and her son Yongkang opened the Yiji Meat Shop at No. 196 Qichang Warehouse Street, Pudong for many years. In order to reduce electricity bills, they cut the outer wire of the electricity meter and stole electricity. On the 7th of last month, they were discovered by the inspectors of the Pudong Electric Company. They immediately reported to the police officer Lin Xiqi to prove it. Because Gu Gao and others firmly denied stealing electricity and falsely accused the company's employees of cutting it and framing them, they reported to the Third District Office of the Public Security Bureau to send Cai Zanzhou to stick a seal on the broken cable. The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau was also asked to inspect and confirm that the wire had been damaged for a long time and there was a possibility of stealing electricity. The company had to strictly punish it because it was a matter of damaging public utilities. On the 18th of last month, it filed a complaint with the Shanghai District Court to investigate and deal with it according to law, and attached a private prosecution, requesting a judgment to recover the electricity bill. After investigation by the prosecutor, it was recognized that the defendants had committed the crime of Article 337, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law and filed a public prosecution. After trial by the judge, the verdict was pronounced on the 19th of this month. Gu Yongkang and Gu Gao were jointly and continuously fined 50 yuan each for theft. If the fine is enforced and not paid, one day of imprisonment will be imposed for each yuan. Gu Yongkang and Gu Gao shall jointly compensate the Pudong Electric Company for the loss of 293 yuan and 24 cents in ocean.

Yangtze River Shanghai Port

Re-setting the New Position of the Floating Buoy 218

The Hydrographic Survey Bureau issued a bulletin for the re-setting of the new position of the floating buoy for hitting ships at the Shanghai port of the Yangtze River Estuary to promote the attention of the shipping industry. The new position of the sixth and seventh sections of the Shanghai port, namely about 121 degrees 30 minutes east longitude and about 31 degrees 15 minutes north latitude. The direction and distance of each floating buoy below are calculated from the flagpole of the Gonghexiang Wharf. The first floating buoy is 202 degrees north, and the distance is 205 chains (every 10 chains is equal to one nautical mile). The second floating buoy is 175 degrees north, and the distance is 1.55 chains. The third floating buoy is 144 degrees north, and the distance is 1.58 chains. The fourth floating buoy is 117 degrees north, and the distance is 2.18 chains.

Medical and Pharmaceutical Circles

The Remarkable Efficacy of Cocklebur Paste in Treating Leprosy 228

Leprosy is prevalent in our country, but effective treatments are scarce. Therefore, once someone is afflicted with leprosy, it is often deemed incurable, causing extreme fear and anxiety. However, the issue is often the medicine not being suited to the ailment, rather than the disease being untreatable. Mr. Zhang Jianyu of Huai'an is a kind and compassionate man well-versed in medicine. He has developed a type of cocklebur paste that is deeply effective in treating leprosy. Fearing the inconvenience of long-distance purchases and shipments, he has made the formula and preparation method publicly available, allowing patients to prepare and make it themselves. If they entrust him to prepare it on their behalf, the price is also reasonable, unlike typical profit-seeking individuals. If impoverished patients are unable to afford the medicine, they can send Mr. Zhang a letter detailing their condition, and he will find a way to donate it to them. He is truly a benefactor of humanity.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong area is partly cloudy to clear, with winds from the northeast to southeast, quite strong and sharp. This area and the middle reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with showers, and there are intermittent but fairly strong easterly winds, caused by a hurricane passing west of Shanghai. The center of the hurricane reached within sixty miles of the intersection of 29 degrees 30 minutes north latitude and 119 degrees 30 minutes east longitude at 2:00 PM yesterday, moving north, with intense winds. Letters to the Editor 231

To the Editor, I read in your newspaper's local news section on the 17th about the arrest of suspects in the red pill case on Xinmin Road, which stated that Chen Laosi was also detained. However, my original name is Chen Yonglin, the fourth child in my family. I have been running the Chen Sen Tai shoe last shop on Xinmin Road for many years, and I have always been law-abiding. On June 10th of this year, I was also elected as a standing committee member of the Shoe Leather Nail Last Trade Association. Qian Baocheng was an apprentice in my shop in 1922, learning the craft. He completed his apprenticeship long ago and has since opened his own Shi Tai shoe last shop. Yonglin and Baocheng have long since been separated. This time, Baocheng was detained because of the red pill case, which has nothing to do with Yonglin. I am writing this special letter to request a correction, for which I would be extremely grateful. Chen Yonglin respectfully bows again, July 21.

To the Esteemed Chief Editor, Greetings. In the local news section of your newspaper on the 19th of this month, there was a news item about the abbot of Dizang Temple, Monk Huilun, being fined for smoking. The facts are not entirely accurate. Our abbot is Zhen Dian and Huilun (also known as Kuanyang) originally resided at the Shangyuan Temple on Mount Jiuhua. He came to Shanghai for business and is staying temporarily at our temple, not as the abbot of our temple. This matter concerns the reputation of our temple. Therefore, we are writing to clarify and request that your newspaper publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section to make a correction, for which we would be most grateful. With best wishes for your well-being, respectfully submitted by the Accounting Department of Dizang Temple, July 21. To the Esteemed Chief Editor of Shen Bao, Greetings. I was delighted to read the news about our delegation's arrival in Shanghai in your newspaper on the 20th of this month. However, the scope of our delegation is very limited. It was organized in accordance with the regulations of the Central Propaganda Committee and has a registered membership. There are a total of fifteen members, all of whom work with the delegation in various locations. There are no delegation members remaining behind. We are concerned that those unaware of the true situation may have doubts or that other improper activities may occur under our name. For the sake of prudence, our delegation respectfully requests that your newspaper publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section. We would be most grateful. With best wishes for your writing, Chen Zhenglong, July 21.
