Errors and Difficulties in Translations 236

|| Reply to Xu Lezhen and Du Luoji ||

Many readers have raised various questions after reading Li Da's translation of "A Course in Materialist Philosophy." We have received three to four hundred questions about this book. Some of these questions are very simple, and we have answered them individually. However, there are also many important questions that we will continue to answer publicly from today onwards. Some of these questions arise because the translation is obscure and difficult for readers to understand. Others are due to typesetting errors. Still others are due to the translator's failure to understand the original meaning and translating it incorrectly. This last point is something we must pay special attention to, because translations in China are generally unreliable. It is inconvenient for readers without careful review, and the review work is also one of the most important things we need to do.

Mr. Xu Zhuzhen asks: 237

1. "Idealist philosophy likes to fight materialism the most, showing that it has become independent from religion." Judging from the preceding sentences, the last sentence here should probably be "showing that it has merged with religion."

Answer: The sentence "Idealist philosophy likes to fight materialism the most..." has been translated incorrectly. The original sentence should be translated as "In order to be able to more effectively fight against materialism, idealist philosophy sometimes pretends to be independent from religion."

2. "But even when based on previously exaggerated scientific propositions, philosophy cannot but pander to religion." This sentence is incomprehensible.

Answer: The sentence "But even when based on one-sided and exaggerated scientific propositions, philosophy cannot but pander to religion" means that idealist philosophers sometimes have to use scientific propositions as their own evidence in order to pretend to be independent of religion. However, the scientific propositions they use are not complete, because in order to suit their needs, they only exaggerate one aspect of the propositions. And in this case, they are still flattering religion and are not really independent.

Mr. Du Luoji asks: 238

1. "Marx in the war era of 1804 to 76..." 1804 must be wrong, please correct it.

Answer: 1804 is a typographical error and should be corrected to 1854.

2. "Qualitative movement, that is, each stage of development, has characteristics that cannot be explained by the laws of development of the previous stage" is completely incomprehensible.

Answer: The development of things must go through many stages, and each stage has its own characteristics. For example, a person must go through the stages of infancy, youth, and middle age from birth to death. At each new stage, this person's character is different from the previous stage. The character of a young person is certainly different from that of an infant. The character of a young person has many new things added compared to an infant. Therefore, the characteristics of the youth stage cannot be explained by the characteristics (or laws of development) of its previous stage (i.e., infancy). Changes in character are qualitative movements.

3. "The will of human beings who are critically thinking" What does this mean? Answer: It means "to think about the will of human beings with a critical attitude." The Populists did not know that the development of society has its own material laws and believed that the future of society could be controlled by the will of human beings. However, this will is not blind, but can only be decided after careful thought and consideration. This will, which has undergone careful thought, is the "will of critical thinking." Of course, the Populists believe that thought and will can control social history, which is a kind of idealistic view of history and is wrong.

4. In the fourth line of the item "Something that is exaggerated in one aspect becomes a fetish and an idol," what does the word "it" refer to? It is best to explain these four lines in detail.

Answer: The two "it" in the seventh line refer to "one aspect" of each aspect.

The "it" in the ninth line refers to "other aspects" besides the aspect in question.

Everything has many aspects. For example, a person generally has physical, mental, and character aspects. In terms of a person's life, infancy, youth, adulthood, and old age are manifestations of the many aspects of a person's development. Since things are multifaceted, each aspect only occupies a part of the importance in that thing and cannot represent the whole of that thing. A person who dies in infancy cannot be considered a complete person. Since each aspect of things cannot become the whole, if we exaggerate one aspect of each aspect, regard this aspect as overly important, and ignore other aspects, so that the other aspects are obscured beneath it and are controlled by it, and we regard it as self-sufficient and independent, and we regard it as an idol, even though it is objectively not that important, but we insist on seeing it as that important, then our meaning cannot be correctly reflected for it, but is a distorted and erroneous reflection. Idealism is the result of exaggerating one aspect of thought. Therefore, idealism is incorrect.

Education News

Ministry of Education Order Regarding Junior Colleges and Above 239

Key points for improvement in all schools (6)

Soochow University, a Private University in Shanghai 240

(1) School of Law: The organization and management of the school is still on track and each item expense are economical, but the following points should be improved

1. Administrative personnel responsible for the school also concurrently hold positions elsewhere, and almost all the faculty are also part-time. This is inappropriate and should be corrected immediately, and full-time faculty and staff should be rehired.

2. The school's graduate school has regulations for master's and doctoral degrees. Before the degree law is promulgated, this provision should be abolished.

3. The evening class is tentatively allowed to continue, but only one enrollment is allowed in the fall each year. The number of enrollments should follow the quota ratio of Category A and B schools stipulated in the Ministry's order. The class time should be advanced and the remedial military training plan should be submitted to the Ministry for approval.

(2) School of Arts and Sciences: The school has been established for a long time and is roughly in scale. All of the measure are still be able to be followed. The biology department has achieved better results with complete equipment. However, the following points should still be improved.

1. The school regulations stipulate that "students who complete a two-year program in the liberal arts can transfer to Nanjing Jinling Theological Seminary for three years, and the school will grant a Bachelor of Arts degree." Jinling Theological Seminary has not been approved by the Ministry for registration. This regulation is inconsistent with the Ministry's regulations and should be terminated immediately. In addition, the pre-medical science department has been cancelled by the Ministry's order and should be discontinued immediately. The original students should be incorporated into the science departments. In addition, the school's regulations on master's degrees have no basis before the degree law is promulgated and should be deleted. 2. The equipment of the physics department of the school of science and engineering urgently needs to be supplemented and faculty should also be added to facilitate teaching.

2. The school and the affiliated middle school are in the same location, which is inconvenient for teaching and training. The affiliated middle school should be separated. The Ministry has already ordered restrictions on the direct admission of graduates of the affiliated middle school to the university. In the future, the school's enrollment should be strictly enforced. Graduates of the affiliated middle school should participate in the entrance examination like graduates of other schools to comply with the law.

3. Special attention should be paid to student training. The accumulated habits of luxury and frivolity must be eliminated as much as possible to make them advocate frugality and tend to the path of academic research.

Chih Tze College, a Private College in Shanghai 241

The founder of the school raised funds to run the school and experienced many difficulties, which shows his enthusiasm. However, there are still many shortcomings in the school's operation. The areas that should be improved are listed on the left.

(1) The school's evening classes were previously ordered to be phased out over the years and should be followed immediately. No more enrollment should be made.

(2) The Department of Law should merge the two departments of political science and economics into a Department of Political Economics from the next academic year.

(3) The total number of students enrolled this year should not exceed 120. The school's past enrollment has been too lenient. In the future, the qualifications of new students should be carefully reviewed and the entrance examination should be strictly enforced.

(4) The work of the two offices of academic affairs and administration is slack. Various statistical forms are missing. They should be thoroughly rectified, administrative reforms should be carried out, and economic transparency should be implemented.

(5) Students at the school are often absent from class. Teachers' leave reached 117 hours in March and April, which is inappropriate. In the future, student absenteeism should be curbed, and teacher absenteeism must be restricted to emphasize academic work. The responsible personnel should check and deal with students whether they are listening carefully in class at any time.

(6) There are too few books and magazines. Funds should be allocated to add them year by year.

(7) Special attention should be paid to student training.

Shanghai College of Law, a Private College 242

Since the school was established a year ago, it has made considerable efforts in the construction of school buildings and the rectification of school affairs. However, the following points still need to be improved.

(1) Supervision of classes, self-study, and examinations should be tightened.

(2) Hire more full-time basic faculty.

(3) Enrich the library, improve its management methods, and promote academic research.

(4) The debts owed by the school should be planned by the school's board of directors to find ways to clear them.

The school is allowed to continue enrollment this year, but each of the two existing departments is only allowed to enroll one class, and the number of students in each class should not exceed 50. The qualifications of new students must be strictly reviewed, and entrance examinations must be held in earnest to improve student level.

Shanghai College of Law and Political Science, a Private College 243

Since the school purchased a new campus site and cleared up debt disputes a year ago, it can be seen that it can still work hard. However, the following points still need to be improved. (1) The school's current school buildings are too narrow and located in a noisy environment, which is not suitable for schools. A new school building should be built on the newly purchased site and completed within one year.

(2) The school's main responsible personnel still have concurrent positions and classes outside the school, which is inappropriate. Although the number of teachers has reportedly increased, in reality, many are still concurrently teaching and working in other schools. In the future, the main personnel should be absolutely restricted from working or teaching outside the school, and teachers should be hired as much as possible who can serve full-time.

(3) The school has always been too lenient in admitting new students. This year, it is tentatively allowed to continue enrollment, but in the next academic year, only one enrollment will be allowed in the fall, and the total number of students in each department should not exceed 90, of which the Department of Law should not exceed 40. The qualifications of new students must be carefully reviewed, and entrance examinations must be strictly held. In addition, the school's Group B should still be terminated in accordance with the previous order and no more enrollment should be made.

(4) The library of the school urgently needs to be enriched. The library fees paid by students should be used to purchase books in full and should not be used to pay the salaries of employees in the library. (5) The number of student absences has reportedly decreased slightly compared with before, but regulations should still be formulated and effectively curbed to eliminate long-standing problems.

(6) Implement strict training to eliminate the previous bad school atmosphere.

Cheng Feng College of Arts, a Private College 244

Since the school was instructed to improve last year, except that the new school building has been started, there has been no progress in other aspects. The main points of the report are again presented, and should be seriously improved.

(1) The school's current school buildings are not suitable for schools. The construction of the new school buildings should be accelerated and completed during the summer vacation this year.

(2) The school has very few books, which are not enough for students to use for reference after class. Funds should be allocated to add them as soon as possible.

(3) The school's important personnel have failed to take effective responsibility, the administration is not on track, school affairs are neglected, and various forms are inaccurate. Most of the teachers are part-time, the treatment is meager, and there are many absences. In the future, the administrative aspect should be thoroughly rectified. Important personnel must be hired as full-time personnel who can take responsibility. Teachers should be based on the principle of full-time and restricted from teaching outside the school. (4) The school's enrollment of new students is too excessive. Students in the school are absent from class at will and without restriction. The level is quite uneven, and there are very few good ones. In the future, the enrollment should be increased to a standard of strict enrollment. Only one enrollment is allowed in the fall each year, and the total number should not exceed 60. The current students should strictly curb absenteeism and train them effectively.

Ministry of Education Interpretation

Limits of Supervision and Guidance of Jointly Established Middle Schools 245

The Ministry of Education previously received a report from the Gansu Education Department that counties often have disputes over the limits of supervision and guidance of jointly established schools, and it is very difficult to handle them in this city because there is no basis. It requested detailed instructions on the standards for dividing the limits of supervision and guidance of jointly established schools. The Ministry once instructed the department, roughly saying that jointly established middle schools should be supervised and guided by the competent administrative organs in the location of the middle school, and matters that the provincial department should report to the jointly established middle school should be forwarded separately by the competent educational administrative organs in the location. When the competent educational administrative organs of the jointly established counties have important instructions for the jointly established middle school, they should jointly issue the instructions to the middle school. The important facilities of the middle school should also be submitted to the competent educational administrative organs of the jointly established counties for approval. It is heard that the situation in the province is similar and an interpretation is requested. It has been instructed by citing the previous situation.

Second Sun Yat-sen Scholarship

Micro-Essays for Physics Competition 248

Total Prize Money: 2,000 Yuan The Sun Yat-sen Cultural and Educational Center's Sun Yat-sen Scholarship this year will focus on the natural science examination and competition in physics. In addition to the previous announcements, the Standing Directors Cai Yuanpei, Zheng Hongnian, Li Zhaohuan, and the appraisal committee members of this year, Ding Xie Lin, Hu Gangfu, Lu Zifang, and others, have successively consulted and decided that the results of the first two categories held last year were inferior, so the decision was made to suspend them temporarily. All prize money will be used for the natural science examination and competition, which will still focus on physics. However, the physics that was rewarded in the previous announcement refers to the academic performance of students in school. This time, the solicitation of essays is to reward graduated students and arouse their interest in specialized research, with the goal of deepening their attainments. The solicitation of essays is divided into two categories: writing and translation. The method is as follows: The total amount of prize money is 2,000 yuan. 1. Writing, Category A Topic (choose one): (1) The Indestructibility of Energy, (2) Photovoltaic Cells and Their Applications, (3) Various Methods for Measuring the Electron Charge E, Category B Prize Money: 1,000 yuan. The top ten will be selected. The first place will receive 400 yuan, the second place will receive 200 yuan, the third place will receive 100 yuan, and the rest will be allocated according to the amount. 2. Translation, Category A Purpose: For university students and middle school teachers to use for reference and self-study, Category B Standard: (1) Short works of considerable value in the history of the development of physics, (2) Small masterpieces that can be used as reference for various theories of physics, (3) Monographs on individual phenomena in physics, (4) Monographs on a certain application problem of physics, Category C Prize Money: 1,000 yuan. The top four will be selected. The first place will receive 400 yuan, the second place will receive 300 yuan, the third place will receive 200 yuan, and the fourth place will receive 100 yuan. The remaining passing manuscripts may be published by the museum on behalf of the translator, and royalties may be drawn as appropriate. The method will be determined separately. 3. Qualifications for Application: Students who have graduated from the Department of Physics of a domestic university. 4. Registration: Applicants must first fill in the registration form in detail and mail it to the Solicitation Department of the Museum at No. 803 Foch Road, Shanghai for registration. 5. Text: Use Chinese. 6. Deadline: The deadline for submitting papers is the end of this year. 7. Announcement: The results will be announced before the winter vacation this year.

City Education Association

Strive to Recover the Right to Education in the Concessions 250

The board of directors passed six improvement measures and requested the Education Bureau and all public organizations to unanimously advocate that the Shanghai Municipal Education Association held its 27th board of directors meeting yesterday. The attendees were Zhang Zhongdao, Xu Zeye, Huang Zaoxiong, Tao Baichuan, Ma Jiazhen, and Chen Jicheng. Zhang Zhongdao chaired the meeting, and Zhang Lichun recorded the minutes. First, Huang Zaoxiong reported on the closing of the people's schools and the student's further education and employment guidance. Then, the matters for discussion were (1) The Eleventh District Education Association requested that the members of the association be mostly gone, and the re-election seemed inappropriate. The fifth executive meeting decided to re-solicit new and old members for a regular re-election. The resolution was approved to follow (2) The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, etc. sent a letter to invite the association to jointly initiate the farewell to the students who will go to Europe and the United States for further study. The resolution was approved and the association participated in the joint initiation and appointed Xu Zeye and Huang Zaoxiong as representatives of the association. (3) The members' meeting of the association resolved to urge the government to recover the right to education in the concessions. Now, five improvement methods for the education in the concessions are proposed for approval. The resolution was approved and submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau and sent to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Concessions, the Private School Coordination Association of the Public Concession, schools at all levels in the Concessions, and various legal public organizations to strive for it together. The meeting adjourned after the discussion. The methods are recorded as follows.

Measures to Improve Education in the Concessions 251

(1) The Chinese Education Office of the Public Concession should be renamed the "Public Concession Bureau of Works Public School Management Office." Its powers should be limited to managing the primary and secondary schools established by the bureau. Administratively, it should be subject to the supervision of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau. As for schools within the concession not established by the Bureau of Works, the Management Office will not interfere. (2) The members of the Private School Subsidy Committee of the Public Concession shall be jointly organized by one-third of the members from the Bureau of Works Education Committee, the Municipal Education Bureau, and the Municipal Education Association.

(3) The school health inspectors employed by the Bureau of Works must no longer be Westerners who do not understand the situation of Chinese schools and have no research on school hygiene. In the future, three Chinese doctors with experience in public health research should be selected, and one of them should be appointed by the Subsidy Committee.

(4) Social education in the concessions seems to be too neglected. The Bureau of Works should allocate funds for social education purposes.

(5) The expenditure of the Bureau of Works on Chinese children's schools should be reduced as much as possible. The funds originally intended by the Bureau of Works to increase Chinese children's schools should be transferred to social education and private school subsidies.

(6) The Municipal Education Bureau should organize a special committee to be responsible for designing and improving education in the concessions.

Sports News

New Tennis Techniques (10) 266

Original by J. PARMLY PARET, Translated by Qian Yiqin and Hong Jun｜Copyright Reserved, No Reproduction Allowed｜

Having discussed the various main ways of forehand strokes, let us now study them in turn, and analyze the various ways to see which one is the most perfect and complete. Usually, the most effective and valuable one seems to be the top-spinning twist from above, because in this way of stroking, the racket is slightly angled upwards, and the swing of the racket is upwards, and the strings brush against the surface of the ball, so the ball flies forward in a spinning way. The benefit of this way is that the ball is spinning forward when it flies forward, so it has a tendency to fall, and it does not fly straight forward. Compared with the straight shot, it lands much faster, so it does not fly out of bounds when stroking heavily.

As for studying why the forward-spinning ball can automatically land, the real reason and the principle of mechanics will be discussed in detail later when discussing the spinning stroke and its effectiveness. Now, just understand that using this method, the ball lands much faster, and there is also a great benefit, that is, when the player hits hard, the ball always lands within the line and does not fly over it.

Because in order to produce the above-mentioned effect, when the player starts to stroke, the forward swing of the racket should be slightly lower than the intended stroke place. When the racket is hitting the ball, the forward swing of the racket should be slightly upward. Some players with excellent skills, they use this method to first swing the racket flat towards the incoming ball. When the strings and the surface of the ball are about to touch, they immediately swing the racket upward and twist the ball hard. Therefore, the ball is brushed by the strings and flies forward in a spinning way.

Regardless of which of the above two methods is adopted, the player should try to make the surface of the ball and the strings have more contact time. The longer the contact time, the more confident the player is in controlling his stroke. If the racket hits the top of the incoming ball, the ball will definitely be difficult to fly over the net. This is very obvious, so when stroking, the racket face should be slightly inclined to meet the top of the incoming ball, and then swing upwards. At this time, the shape of the racket is of course with the bottom edge backward and the top edge forward.

The most important part of applying this method is that after the ball has been hit, the swing of the racket should be made as smoothly as possible. Do not try too hard to twist the ball and stop the swing, because in order to make the ball fly forward in a spinning way, and to shorten its flight path, you must swing the racket all the way over your left shoulder. To shorten its flight path, you must still swing the racket head over your neck smoothly. Therefore, after the ball has left the strings, the wrist should be relaxed immediately. When the upper arm swings across the chest, the racket head must pass over the left shoulder, and the power of the racket will automatically stop, and there is no need to use wrist strength to stop it.

Speaking of the benefits of this method, in addition to the above-mentioned - the ball spins forward, lands faster, and can be stroked hard without flying over the line - there are even greater benefits, because the ball spins forward and lands quickly, so its rebound force must be stronger and farther. In this case, the opponent has no choice but to retreat backwards to meet it. Furthermore, this method makes the ball fly faster in the air than the undercutting method, and the ball spins forward quickly, making it difficult for the opponent to intercept it effectively.

At this time, the opponent has two disadvantages when intercepting the incoming ball, one is that the ball is spinning forward and will immediately fall down when it flies over the net. If this method is used properly, the ball must already be very low when it flies to the opponent's side. He must slowly lift the ball over the net to intercept it. At this time, the spinning force of the ball will shoot slightly obliquely upwards when it comes into contact with his racket. Secondly, when encountering an opponent who is good at intercepting, although the ball in his hand will not shoot upwards obliquely, the method of stroking must be slow, and the flight path of the ball must be slightly higher, making it easy to deal with. This is also a very obvious benefit.

However, there is also a great danger in using this method, that is, the player often has a tendency to try too hard to make the ball spin, thus forgetting the insufficient forward thrusting force when stroking, so that the ball cannot fly into the opponent quickly and deeply. This type of stroke cannot be used for impact. Practice until the contact between the strings and the ball can be longer, and when contacting, a sweeping motion is used to generate the rotation. After stroking, the ball immediately leaves the racket quickly. This is very obvious, but if more sweeping motion is used and less impact motion is used when stroking, the contact between the ball and the racket can naturally be extended. British players are more skilled in this method, and when they meet the incoming ball, the racket is swept out flat. When the surface of the ball is in contact with the strings and has not left, the wrist takes advantage of the momentum to turn, thus generating the force for the ball to spin forward.

Page 16

Women's Garden

On Freedom of Marriage 276

— Fei

Since the opening of maritime restrictions and the eastward spread of Western culture, the clamor for freedom of marriage has shaken our "parents' command" and "matchmaker's words" – the "marry a chicken, follow the chicken; marry a dog, follow the dog" style marriage rules. Following the "Xinhai" Revolution, some reformist men and women raised the banner of rebellion, practicing autonomous marriage. By the time of the "May Fourth" Movement, the discussion on freedom of marriage and even freedom of love had reached a theoretical dead end; it had become a conclusion: marriage should be free, and love should be free! Who knew that after the so-called "National Revolution" surged up from the "May Thirtieth" Movement, it has been seven or eight years, and we still see news in the newspapers every day about young people forced into arranged marriages committing suicide, especially women! How can this be? We truly cannot help but feel a sense of "What kind of world is this!"

However, looking at the current laws, in the Civil Code, Book Four, Chapter Two, "Marriage" section, there are clearly such provisions:

Section 1: Engagement

Article 972: Engagement should be entered into independently by the man and woman involved.

Article 973: A man under the age of seventeen or a woman under the age of fifteen may not enter into an engagement.

Article 774: Minors of either sex entering into an engagement must obtain the consent of their legal guardian.

Article 975: Engagement may not be enforced by coercion.

This was promulgated by the National Government on December 26th of the 19th year and implemented on May 5th of the 20th year! It seems not to be a bounced check. However, what is publicized in the newspapers is not just the suicide by well-throwing of Shi Jihua, a student at the Hangxing Elementary Girls' School; or the collective drowning death of nine women in Hui'an, Fujian; even in the capital, Nanjing, in the same month of June, there was a Li Lianlin who, opposing an arranged marriage, swore to death that she would not marry. Unable to withstand the coercion of her stubborn father, she took sleeping pills and died! (See the Nanjing Dihua Evening News of June 3rd.) Why is it that so many young women have died, and yet it is "unseen and unheard"? The current Criminal Code, Book One, Chapter Twenty-Five, "Crimes Against Freedom," also clearly has the following provisions:

Article 318: Anyone who uses violence or coercion to compel another to do something they are not obligated to do, or obstructs another from exercising their rights, shall be sentenced to imprisonment for a term of no more than three years, detention, or a fine of no more than three hundred yuan.

Attempted crimes under this article shall be punished.

Article 319: Anyone who threatens another with harm to their life, body, freedom, reputation, or property, causing danger to their safety, shall be sentenced to imprisonment for a term of no more than three years, detention, or a fine of no more than three hundred yuan.

May I ask: Doesn't despotic arranged marriage, and even the coercion to enforce it, constitute a violation of the "crimes against freedom" in the criminal law – especially the two articles cited above? All citizens are equal before the law of the country! In theory and according to the law, it doesn't matter who is the parent and who is the child! However, what is most incomprehensible is that the suicides of women in Hangzhou and Fujian in opposition to despotic marriages can still be said to be cases where their parents did not exert obvious coercion, while in the death of Li Lianlin in Nanjing, her father's coercion was extremely evident. Why do we not see prosecutors "investigating" and "prosecuting"? Is it that young women are not protected by the laws of the country, and that parents can arbitrarily decide their life and death? Regarding this truth, we hope to receive a public and detailed explanation from the "legislative" and "judicial" organs! At the same time, we also hope that lawyers who pride themselves on protecting human rights and legal interests can give us some brilliant and correct opinions on "legal texts," "legal principles," and "precedents"!

Furthermore, regarding this issue – the victory of freedom of marriage – although the specter of feudalism is still active everywhere, I believe it is not a very difficult matter. For example, before the "Xinhai" Revolution, parents and other elder relatives could execute their children at will, which was not prohibited by law. Later, the law was revised, and killing children (regardless of whether they were disobedient or disgraced the family) was the same as committing murder. In the past twenty-odd years, such incidents have been rare. Autonomous marriage, the Civil Code clearly stipulates that it should be entered into independently by the parties involved, and also stipulates that it may not be enforced by coercion! Moreover, in the Criminal Code, there are provisions on "crimes against freedom" that can be relied upon for redress and relief! Laws are not bounced checks after all. If everyone publicizes them and applies them, their effectiveness will be substantial! The times are advancing after all. If everyone knows the truth of the "current law," who would willingly do such a stupid thing that harms their children and violates the national law? Speaking of this, I hope that future school education should provide students with legal knowledge so that young women in general know how to use the law and do not die unjustly.

Women and Cinema 277

— Caoling

According to the general observation of ticket collectors at theaters, about 50% of moviegoers are women. According to the conversation with people in charge of film companies, there are always several letters written by women every day asking to be actors. From these two perspectives, we can confirm that women and cinema have an interactive relationship.

Indeed, the film industry in China is a new and promising enterprise. It is a powerful new force in Chinese culture. It has a significant mission: its future fate and prosperity are of great importance to the future of Chinese culture! On the one hand, it is an excellent phenomenon for women to bravely participate in this new cultural movement – which is, of course, also a new path for women's liberation and independent women's occupations – or to support this movement.

But reality is the proof of theory, and reality will show all the ugly phenomena to everyone. What are the women who are now engaged in the film industry like? What is the attitude of the women (phenomenon) who are now supporting this new cultural movement?

Obviously, the new film industry has been tainted by the individual irregular actions of a small number of female employees (that is, the wrong actions taken by those who do not truly understand film but are engaged in it). Of course, I would never say here that the ugliness of the entire film industry stems from this point, but I don't think anyone would deny that if a small part of an entire industry is not on the right track, it will inevitably restrain or affect the whole. The poor state of the film industry has more significant reasons than this, but the female employees' ignorance of the cultural mission of film, as well as their actions that do not cherish themselves, and the dishonor they find for themselves, will inevitably affect the progress of the entire film movement. On the other hand, the fact that very meaningful and good films are not welcomed by women clearly shows that women do not truly understand "film art" and are not truly supporting "film art."

Of course, the past is the past. The future of Chinese film art has great hope. At the same time, Chinese film art urgently needs women who understand it to bravely participate, pioneer, and support it!

We will never deny that participating in the film industry is a new profession for women with a cultural mission. At the same time, we will never hesitate to think that the time for understanding and supporting film culture has not yet arrived.

For the sake of the early realization of good phenomena, we must put forward the following specific opinions.

1. We hope that all high schools and above (coeducational) have theoretical courses on film so that people can understand "film art" a little more.

2. We hope that there is a specialized film department in a certain school. Especially for women. Because the general phenomenon now is that the intellectual level of female film employees is lower than that of male employees.

These are preventive suggestions.

1. Standing on the standpoint of women's liberation itself, we should expose the shortcomings of female film employees.

2. We should eliminate all the evil environments and forces that tempt female film employees to fall into depravity.

3. Women's publications should have simple theories or introductions about film.

On Women (Continued) 278

— Gorky, translated by Wan Qimei

IV

Seeing is not as good as knowing, and the basis of knowledge is labor experience, not "speculation." Perhaps men see more than women, but their knowledge is limited to the narrow skills of how hunters kill animals.

Women settle down, and their knowledge accumulation process gradually develops due to the protection of life, health, increasing food, and improving working conditions. What is most noteworthy is that religious historians have said almost nothing about the role women played in the formation of religious rituals.

Generally, the creators of religious ideas were the old men watching the stove. Although they had lost their ability to work, they had rich experience in killing wild animals and knowledge of the principles of corporate action. Therefore, these old men were the authority in the hunting tribe.

It should be pointed out in passing that religious researchers always underestimate the role of water and fire in stimulating the imagination. Fire is a majestic but lovely force. It has a vibrant power and an unyielding desire to burn. It has dazzling beauty and agile action. It has a pleasant skill in making meat more delicious. It can turn trees into ashes, smash stones, and sometimes turn stones into liquid. It can destroy water, make water boil and turn into gas. In short, fire, this diverse and strange force, undoubtedly and powerfully influenced the development of primitive people's imagination. Water probably has the same effect. People see water everywhere: their bodies also have water; wet trees also evaporate water when burning; in the water flow, people can see their shadows, although the water is flowing, it does not wash away his shadow; water meets fire, either water destroys fire, or water is destroyed by fire and turns into gas and rises; sometimes meteors and lightning are found in the sky. All these things, people have seen, but as mentioned above, there is a big difference between seeing and knowing. A religious thinker, someone like Sha, Luo Weifu, etc., gave a definition of the ability to see, saying that the occurrence of seeing seems to be unrelated to human reason, and is not subordinate to the phenomena of the real world, he created another divine world.

To add this ability to primitive humans is to put primitive people together with Swedenborg and other illusionists. Primitive people are personal anthropomorphists. When they begin to consciously treat natural phenomena, they find similarities with themselves in nature. At that time, people fought for nature and did not need metaphysics. Primitive people did not respect nature as God, but only "according to their own image" "viewed nature as a soul". Therefore, primitive people used magic to fight against nature. At that time, sorcery and witchcraft were not metaphysical.

What bourgeois cultural historians care about is not to reveal the true meaning of facts, they only select materials for preconceived conclusions. What they find in the prehistoric past is not the cultural founders that archeology and ethnography tell us – ancient laborers, but the "companions" of these people – gods, without gods, primitive people seem unable to live.

The need for metaphysics is not for fighting against nature, but for opposing people. The occurrence of theism is not out of the joyous motives of ancient religious historians, but out of the priests' ambition to defend their rule over people. Needless to say, it is very difficult to trace the development of realistic ideas that are inspired by the process of people's labor and life struggles.

The study of primitive culture began in the eighteenth century, and the research materials have undergone countless changes in thousands of years due to the complex mixture of concepts of various tribes and races.

Assuming that people, based on practice, have already had a kind of "foreknowledge" that can overcome nature, and regard themselves as heroes, great men, and even gods, this still does not mean metaphysics or the supernatural, because the "Olympus" gods are completely real "nobles," and the "Edda" gods are just typical Norwegian farmers. The gods of general cults are mostly idealized typical craftsmen. (Later deleted) (End of this section, the whole article is not finished)

After Reading Biwuwu's "On Adultery and Murder" 279

— Hao Yu

Today, I opened the newspaper and read Biwuwu's article "On Adultery and Murder", and I couldn't help but feel emotional. Adultery and murder is indeed a criminal act, which is inexcusable in law and morality.

The act of killing, no matter whether its motive is revenge, love, or adultery, is not allowed by law. As long as you kill someone, or attempt to kill someone, you deserve to be punished. Adultery and murder is not protected or defended by any law. Therefore, we understand that this matter of adultery and murder is difficult to eradicate even with the most severe laws, just like other murder cases.

Biwuwu said: "Under the prevention of propriety, women are willing to risk death to communicate a little affection with other men, and her married life is undoubtedly not satisfactory; and the reason for that dissatisfaction is often because the husband has an affair. In this situation, who should die?" I think no one should die. Because this kind of illicit affair is wrong for everyone. The wife has an affair with another man, and that man is also someone else's husband; at the same time, her own husband has an affair with another woman, which is just like she has an affair with another man, so I think that the man killing his wife, or the woman poisoning her husband, is equally wrong. If couples cannot communicate with each other, and even cannot spend the night together, then what kind of couple is that? It is better to be frank and each be with the person who is able to communicate with each other.

However, in today's society, the minds of most people are still bound by propriety, and the remnants of feudalism have not been eliminated. People inevitably look down on divorced people – especially women. Therefore, there are many couples in name only – who are actually unhappy couples – who dare not easily file for divorce; another reason is that for couples who file for divorce, the man has to bear a sum of alimony that he cannot afford, so he would rather the couple hate each other than get a divorce. The result is that they end up trying to commit suicide, or having affairs with others, and all kinds of unfortunate things happen. Why bother? If couples cannot feel any interest in each other, they should leave. It is better to reconcile when either party realizes that they were wrong in the future, which is more refreshing than a hypocritical couple suffering mental pain. Moreover, forcing things to continue can really make the broken relationship more and more rigid, to the point where it cannot be salvaged.

Although that's what I said, can society allow us to act so freely? There are now many freely divorced people who are subject to much criticism and discrimination. No wonder so many unhappy couples would rather endure mental pain and continue to support themselves, while seeking lovers elsewhere; doesn't such behavior receive social criticism and condemnation? However, we must know: society is organized by people, and divorce and affairs are done by people; criticism and condemnation are also done by people. Since they are both things done by people, why should we scold ourselves? If we think that free marriage is legal, why is free divorce not legal? What is there to criticize? What is there to condemn? Social affairs are all behaviors of people. If the current society allows people to marry and divorce freely, there is no need to condemn the divorce of others; if someone wants to condemn, those people are not people of the current society, but people of the previous century, they are zombies, what do we people of the current society fear from them?

The Simplest and Most Accurate Pregnancy Prediction Method: 23.7, 8 280

— Wu

There have been two or three methods for predicting pregnancy, but they are all very troublesome and not very accurate. Recently, Dr. Fukushima of Kumamoto Medical University in Japan has newly invented a very simple prediction method. This method is quite consistent with scientific principles, and the results of the doctor's experiments are actually very accurate. Now I will introduce it below.

Diagnosis method

You can put the pregnant woman's urine in a glass tube, add a few drops of bromine water, and after ten minutes, add a few drops of a mixture of strong ammonia water and ammonium carbonate water, and shake it slightly. The urine of a pregnant woman contains a large amount of Histidine, so the urine will turn pink. If it is said that it is not pregnant, then it will not change color. This is just using the hydrolysis of Histidine, so the procedure is very simple.

Confirmation

Dr. Fukushima used this method to conduct experiments on women in the attached hospital of the school. Among the fifty women who were asked to pre-diagnose pregnancy, forty-six were positive (i.e., changed color) and four were negative. The results were very accurate. Then, he tested dozens of ordinary healthy women (non-pregnant women), and most of them were negative (i.e., no discoloration). From this, it can be seen that this method can be used in practice.

"Autumn Wind, Autumn Rain Sadden People to Death" 281

— Fangshiren

In this year's summer, when the rain shadows are vague, the heat waves are high, and the land is cracking everywhere, reading the publications commemorating Ms. Qiu Jin, I can't help but feel a burst of coolness and comfort. Recalling the morning of the sixth day of the sixth lunar month in the old calendar of 1907, a hero devoted to the racial revolution, the female knight Qiu Jin, after being arrested, before being killed at Xuetingkou in Shaoxing, the only confession she wrote to the plague official, who was even more ferocious than a beast, was just the terse sentence "Autumn rain, autumn wind, all kill people." Can we not feel a stream of sadness and magnificence surging into our hearts?

Although she was born in a bureaucratic family in Shaoxing, Zhejiang, and later became the daughter-in-law of a wealthy gentry in Xiangtan, Qiu Jin was always the epitome of a most progressive new woman in a specific era and specific society. She was a round of blazing summer sun that broke through the old atmosphere of sorrowful autumn rain and autumn wind! Seeing her take off her gorgeous clothes and jewelry and run to Japan to study, she immediately joined the Tongmenghui: after returning to China, she lived in Houdeli, Hongkou, Shanghai, and made explosives with her comrades. The medicine exploded, and she was injured. In addition, she was almost caught by the police and went to jail. After that, under severe oppression, she secretly organized the anti-Qing Restoration Army. Finally, she was arrested after being betrayed, but despite suffering all kinds of punishments that we can imagine, the only confession of this solid and strong female warrior was still "Autumn rain, autumn wind, all kill people"! Although she belonged to the previous generation of women, her courageous spirit has turned the degenerate modern ladies of the contemporary era decades later into shameless goblins!

Singing "The Yellow River originates from the Zhejiang tide, guarding my Chinese Han heroes, do not let the Manchurian barbarians leave a piece of armor, the Xuanyuan God is a natural pride", Qiu Jin, from the perspective of Hua Mulan who "bid farewell to the Yellow River in the morning, and slept in the Blackwater in the evening, did not hear the voice of her parents calling her daughter, but only heard the sound of the Yan Mountain Hu cavalry whining", must be incredibly great. Indeed, from the narrow family affection of flesh and blood, and setting out to join the army on behalf of her father, Hua Mulan, to Qiu Jin who organized the so-called Restoration Army for the people and for the Han people, in between, the progress of the new woman is immeasurable.

Of course! Qiu Jin, who advocated "restoring the Han people and greatly revitalizing national power", seems ridiculously narrow from the perspective of the new soldiers in the current national liberation movement! But this is the era that restricts her. She has made the greatest and best efforts to fulfill the task that the era imposed on her. If, in the current stage of the Chinese national liberation movement, there are still people singing the old tunes of "restoring the Han people and greatly revitalizing national power", or preparing for the massacre of nation against nation, then the ghost of Qiu Jin, who is lying in a solitary tomb by the West Lake, will never be able to rest in peace!

Autumn rain and autumn wind are always so sad, but where are the new women like Qiu Jin who wave flags and shout to sweep away this evil atmosphere?

The Sex Knowledge That Women Should Have (Continued) 282

— Liang

(2) Positions during intercourse

Generally, young men often ask their partners to take one or several abnormal positions (sitting or standing, etc.) during intercourse, causing some women to develop diseases that damage the vagina even after being married for several years or having given birth several times. Especially for those whose reproductive organs are unbalanced, it is easier to cause cracks in the posterior fornix of the vagina, which causes the same symptoms as those mentioned above. This also needs attention.

(3) Abstaining from intercourse during menstruation

Women's libido is at its highest during menstruation (especially at the end of it): however, intercourse is absolutely forbidden during menstruation. Because menstruation is a manifestation of the destruction and bleeding of the uterine mucosa, which is the same as a uterine injury. If you have intercourse during menstruation, it is tantamount to giving bacteria a chance to invade the uterus, causing endometritis, peritonitis, and other diseases. Moreover, the physical stimulation during intercourse can easily cause the danger of bleeding. At the same time, men are also prone to urethritis, pseudo-gonorrhea, and other diseases.

(4) Restrictions on intercourse during pregnancy

Some medical experts advocate absolutely stopping intercourse during pregnancy, which may be an extreme view. However, intercourse during pregnancy must be limited. In the first half of pregnancy, it is okay to have moderate intercourse - the most important thing about moderation is to avoid excessive sexual excitement, excessive exertion, and heavy pressure on the abdomen, to prevent uterine bleeding and miscarriage. As for the second half of pregnancy, especially the last two months, intercourse must be prohibited; otherwise, uterine bleeding, premature rupture of the amniotic membrane, premature birth, and fever after childbirth may occur.

(5) Cleaning after intercourse

Many Chinese women suffer from leucorrhea, and the reason for this is mostly due to the lack of cleanliness of the reproductive organs; because of its uncleanness, it causes uterine diseases. Therefore, keeping the reproductive organs clean is the only good way to reduce women's diseases, especially after intercourse, it must be thoroughly washed. The washing is best done half an hour after the event. The method is: use a vaginal irrigator filled with lukewarm liquid, insert it into the cavity and wash it. The liquid, such as one percent carbolic acid, two percent Lysol, or boiled and sterilized saline, can be used. (The End)

Abstract of Laws and Regulations 283

Civil Law Section 2: Marriage

Article 980: A man under the age of eighteen or a woman under the age of sixteen shall not marry.

Article 981: A minor shall obtain the consent of their legal guardian to marry.

Article 982: Marriage shall have a public ceremony and two or more witnesses.

Article 983: Marriage is not permitted with the following relatives.

1. Lineal relatives by blood and lineal relatives by marriage.

2. Collateral relatives by blood and collateral relatives by marriage of different generations, but this restriction does not apply to collateral relatives by blood beyond the eighth degree of kinship or collateral relatives by marriage beyond the fifth degree of kinship.

3. Collateral relatives by blood of the same generation within the eighth degree of kinship, but this restriction does not apply to cousins.

The restrictions on marriage of relatives by marriage in the preceding paragraph shall also apply after the termination of the relationship of relatives by marriage.

Article 984: A guardian and a ward shall not marry during the subsistence of the guardianship relationship. However, this restriction does not apply with the consent of the ward's parents.

Article 985: A person with a spouse shall not remarry.

Research on Fireflies 289

— Zhang Nancun

Hai'er saw the firefly light flickering and felt it was very strange, so he asked his mother: "It is unique among animals that fireflies can emit light. The flickering situation is like an electrical discharge in the air. I wonder if it can discharge electricity?"

Mother said: "It is not electricity. The firefly has a light-emitting organ at the end of its tail. When breathing, air enters, and a biochemical reaction occurs, so it flashes on and off. If there was electricity, wouldn't people get an electric shock if they caught a firefly? It lays its eggs on aquatic plants in summer. Fireflies gather more near the water than elsewhere. Therefore, there is the idiom 'rotten grass turns into fireflies.' Scholars in ancient times were diligent and studied by the light of fireflies in pouches at night, which is praised as a good story. In the past, when Emperor Yang of Sui traveled to Yangzhou via the Grand Canal, he ordered the people along the way to catch countless fireflies and present them to him. At night, he released them on both sides of the river. Thousands of groups flew in the trees, like 'fire trees and silver flowers,' which was very beautiful. He really came up with this playful idea, but Emperor Yang of Sui was extravagant and dissolute, and soon he was 'killed and the country was destroyed.'"

Hai'er asked again: "Light can generate heat, and biochemical reactions require burning. Why doesn't it burn and die?"

Mother said: "There is liquid contained in the firefly's tail. The water in the liquid combines with light gas, which does not support combustion, so there is no danger of burning. This is its physiological function."

Hai'er asked again: "If fireflies don't discharge electricity, are there any other benefits?"

Mother said: "Fireflies and their larvae eat all kinds of pests, which is beneficial to agriculture. Don't swat them with a fan when you see them. Let them fly freely and work to eliminate pests for farmers, which is also a virtue of 'cherishing things.'"

Summer Games 290

— Ding He

In summer, because the sun is very hot on the body, many children hide in their houses and don't go out to play. But isn't it too lonely to sit in the house?

Yes, because you children are too lonely, so I will tell you about several games to play in the summer, and they are all very interesting. Try playing according to the following methods, is it very interesting?

Flying Bubbles Playing this game is best in two locations, one, under an electric fan. One, in the sunlight, because these two places can increase your interest in playing.

Before starting the game, prepare a bowl or a bottle, and a wheat straw or a bamboo pen holder. Put half a bowl of water in the bowl, add some soap shavings to the water, and stir it with chopsticks until the soap shavings disappear, then you can start playing this game.

The method of playing is to hold one end of the wheat straw in your mouth and extend the other end into the bowl. As soon as the end extending into the bowl touches the water, take it out, and then gently blow on the end held in your mouth. A very small bubble will appear on the other end of the straw, and slowly become bigger, then it will fall off the end of the straw and float in the air. When there is wind, it can also fly up and down.

If you play this game under an electric fan, it can fly back and forth, up and down. If you play it in the sunlight, it will become colorful bubbles.

Finding the Doll First, I want to tell you that you only need two people to play this game, dividing who is A and who is B.

Now, let A find it for B first: A's right middle finger represents the doll, A's left hand tightly grips A's right fingers, only revealing the fingertip, but A must make it so that B can't tell which one is the doll and which one isn't, and then let B find it.

B finds the doll among the five fingers. Once B finds it, B uses their finger to pinch the doll tightly, and tells A to open their left hand to see if B has found it or not. If B found it, A loses and B wins. A opens their hand for B to hit their palm. While hitting, B sings the following song:

"Find the doll, look for the doll, the doll is lost in the big river. Cannot scoop it out, cannot climb up; the doll cries and says, I will hit your palm thirty-six times: one, two, three, four, five..."

If B doesn't find it and picks the wrong one, then switch and let B do it for A, and continue in this way.

P>Children's Science Lecture: Terrible Mosquitoes and Flies

— Lin Yin

Summer has arrived, the weather is hot, and terrible mosquitoes and flies are everywhere. Little friends, do you all think they are terrible? Yes, they are pests. But does everyone know where their harm lies? What methods can be used to get rid of them? I will now briefly tell you.

Mosquitoes hatch in sewage, warmed by the sun and hatched into "larvae." (Figure 1) When they shed their skin and their bodies become curved, they become pupae (Figure 2). Then, when they grow legs and wings, the pupa splits the line in the center of its back, and the mosquito flies out. (Figure 3) Male mosquitoes eat grass juice, and female mosquitoes suck human blood. We hate them very much, and after they suck the blood of patients, they spread diseases to us. There is also a type of malarial mosquito, which always points its tail upwards when it rests. (Figure 4) It is the medium for spreading malaria (chills and fever), and it is even more hateful.

Fly eggs are produced in rotten food, and become maggots, which are larvae, overnight. (Figure 5) After ten days, they shed their skin, shrink inside, become oval, and become pupae. (Figure 6) After another three to several days, they grow wings and feet, break out of the shell, and become flies. (Figure 7) Its habits are that it likes dirt. It has three pairs of legs, and each leg grows countless fine hairs. Each fine hair on each leg can hold at least one million microorganisms, so if we eat food that flies have gathered on, we will definitely have a stomachache or diarrhea, because it brings the germs from its feet to our food.

Mosquitoes and flies are our enemies. They can make us sick, even die, so we should find ways to kill them. The method of extermination is fundamentally cleanliness, such as eliminating sewage and dirt, cleaning utensils, etc. If mosquitoes and flies have already been found, mosquito coils, flypaper, fly swatters, fly traps, etc. can be used to exterminate them. (Figure 8) Flypaper is made by frying rosin, tung oil, and honey and applying them to thick hemp paper. The method of making a fly swatter is also very simple. Prepare lead gauze, bamboo strips, and lead wire, and you can make it as shown in (Figure 9).

— Yi'an

How to Pass the Summer Vacation? 292

— Bo Zhen

The sunspots are gradually shrinking, and the heat is increasing day by day, always hovering around 100 degrees on the thermometer.

Little friends, are you bored at home? When you want to go out and play, your parents don't allow you to go out, fearing that the scorching sun will damage your body. It can be seen that parents' love for their children is so profound!

Reading and writing at home for two or three hours is enough. If you read and write too much, your brain will become dizzy. How should you spend the remaining time?

Now is an era of scientific prosperity, and you should do some scientific toys to play with to suit the trend. I can introduce you to:

(1) Periscope:

Materials: wooden boards, glass, saw, ruler, pencil.

Method: First saw the wooden board into a cube about eight inches long and two inches wide. Open a square hole two inches away from each end. At the same time, apply ink to the two pieces of glass and fit them exactly in the center of the square holes, forming an angle of about 45 degrees, and it is done. (As shown in Figure 1)

How to play: Extend the top of the mirror out of the corner of the wall or the gap in the door. Aim the square hole at the top of the mirror at the destination you want to peek at, and then look at the glass through the square hole at the bottom of the mirror, and you can see the things outside in the glass.

Two Sailing Boat:

Materials: wooden board, bamboo chopsticks, card paper, saw, pencil, ruler, nails, scissors, thread.

Method: Take a piece of wooden board five or six inches long, two or three inches wide, and four or five minutes thick. Saw one end into a pointed head and the other end into a round shape. Use a long piece of wood as the keel and nail it to the bottom of the boat. Nail a nail on the keel to give the boat a center of gravity so that it can be stable. At the same time, use two bamboo chopsticks to make a mast, and punch two small holes in the hull. Insert the mast into the two small holes. At the same time, cut out four rectangular pieces of card paper and thread them onto the bamboo mast as sails, and it is done. (As shown in Figure 2)

Little friends, if you want it to move forward by itself without relying on wind power. Then just saw the round end into a concave shape, put a piece of cowhide tendon on the left and right ends of the concave shape, and then saw a piece of wood smaller than the concave shape, embed it in the middle of the cowhide tendon, wind the small piece of wood tightly, and put it in the water, and it can move forward by splashing water. (As shown in Figure 3)

How to play: Put it in a narrow and long water swamp, and when a gust of wind blows, the sailboat will proceed very steadily and quickly.

Children Around the World (2) 294

— Xiao Jianqing

(5) These are children from Siberia. Siberia is in the north of Asia. The weather is very cold. The children there wear very thick leather clothes and hats and do all kinds of games on the snow to keep warm.

(6) These are children from Mongolia in our country. They live in a place with many deserts. They like to live a pastoral life, so they are good at riding horses and are very strong.

(7) These children were born in the Ryukyu Islands, and were originally our compatriots, but later Japan snatched the Ryukyus. Now they are small slaves of the Japanese. Children! We must aspire to help them escape from the sea of suffering.

(8) Children, do you know this child? They are Japanese, and from an early age they have received a robber-like education, preparing to rob the places of weak nations when they grow up. Children, be prepared and resist them!

Grain

Many Opportunities for Flour Prices to Rise 309

Recently, there have been movements in the northern Manchuria water situation… Tianjin and Yingkou are taking action

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, foreign wheat quotations showed a fall of 0.6 jiao in Chicago and about 0.5 jiao in Canada. Moreover, this port continued to see timely rain, which was quite sufficient. Therefore, after the opening prices, the prices of each month had slightly retreated by 0.5-1 fen compared to the previous day. However, the market sentiment remained firm, mainly because the northern Manchuria area was suffering from flooding, and the demand for flour was feared to increase step by step. Therefore, groups from Yingkou, Andong, and Tianjin kept buying actively. This month, because there were spot goods available for drawing, buying was even more intense. Therefore, after the second session, the market for each month rebounded again. The reason for this rise was first due to the great drought, which led to outside traders actively hoarding, and then the great flood in northern Manchuria, which led to actual sales. Therefore, although foreign wheat was quoted lower, and timely rain continued to fall, the turbulent flood ultimately failed to relieve the urgent need. Subsequent observations indicate that since the trend has no entered a regular pattern, there is bound to be a continuing risk of further rise. As a result, this month's rose another 0.4 fen, August's rose 0.2 fen, September's rose 0.075 fen, and October to December's rose 0.2 fen.

Wheat Futures Buyers in Strong Force 310

Yesterday's wheat futures market, after the opening in the morning, the markets for each month initially fell and then rose. Foreign wheat quotations retreated by varying degrees of 0.5-0.6 jiao, and the tense situation inevitably eased, as timely rain was received everywhere. Therefore, the opening prices for each month fell by varying degrees of 0.1-0.3 fen compared to the previous day. Later, because the flour market recovered from sluggishness to briskness, and outside large accounts actively purchased again, the markets after the opening became brisk again. Although the rising trend was not as strong as the previous day, the transactions for each month were exceptionally brisk. Subsequent observations indicate that natural disasters of floods and droughts continue to prevail, and the feared deterioration in the future is easily incited by speculators. As a result, this month was unchanged, August improved by 0.5 fen, September to November improved by 0.4 fen, and December improved by 0.6 fen. The spot wheat market received continuous arrivals, and sales were also brisk, generally being sold as soon as they arrived and unable to accumulate. Prices were better by 0.2-0.3 fen compared to the previous day. Open prices: Mingguang, Suzhou, and Bengbu wheat at 3.37 yuan, Linhuai guan wheat at 3.38 yuan, Hefei wheat at 3.17 yuan, Qingjiang wheat at 3.35 yuan, Shandong wheat at 3.4 yuan, Liuhe wheat at 3.25 yuan, Gaotong wheat at 3.33 yuan, Taizhou wheat at 3.32 yuan, Jiangjiaba wheat at 3.36 yuan, Yangzhou wheat at 3.33 yuan, Gaoyou wheat at 3.25 yuan, and Bianjiang wheat at 3.13 yuan. Oil Market: White Tung Oil, Supposed to Sell Well, Isn't Selling 316

Tung oil is normally a fast-selling item in the summer. However, due to foreign firms’ demand, white tung oil sales continue throughout the year, so there's no distinction between peak and off-seasons. Recently, foreign firms in Hankou have slightly reduced their purchases, and the selling price has fallen to 28.60 or 28.70 yuan. Although the market appears weak, prices are not expected to fall much further. Therefore, the price of Xiangtung oil from Hankou remains around 24 yuan. Generally, if foreign firms do not resume purchases, prices may stabilize. However, if there are large-scale transactions, prices will likely rise again. Thus, the market for white tung oil is fluctuating. The situation for domestic-selling Hongxiu tung oil is different. The prolonged drought has had a significant impact. Farmers are busy working in the fields, constantly drawing water for irrigation, and have no time to pay attention to painting utensils. As a result, the sale of Hong oil is not happening during the season, due to the weather. Fortunately, the production of Hongjiang oil this year has been greatly reduced, so even though sales are sluggish, the market has been able to maintain itself. Seeing the small production volume earlier, those engaged in this business were worried about shortages during the sales season. But they have unexpectedly been spared by the drought, allowing them to cope adequately. Recently, prices remain unchanged: Jichang and Zheng Hong are at 28 yuan per barrel, Jiyingfeng at 26.8 yuan, and deputy Hong Yang Hengyuan Qingyuanfeng at 24 yuan. Jifeng Yingtong Taifeng is at 23.40 or 23.50 yuan.
